### [1] [StereoSplat+: Feed-Forward Stereo Gaussian Splatting with Diffusion-Assisted Progressive Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08808)
*Zihua Liu,Masatoshi Okutomi*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: StereoSplat+ 是一种基于扩散模型的前馈框架，可从单个立体图像对中实现因果重建。它通过 StereoSplat 模块融合成本体积与三平面3D体积分支，利用连续姿态编码实现跨视角数量和相机配置的泛化；再结合扩散增强的一次性渐进推理机制，通过生成新视图并反馈优化3DGS，显著提升在遮挡区域和强视图外推下的渲染质量与几何精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有3D高斯溅射（3DGS）方法依赖多视角观测或非因果未来帧访问，难以应用于受限于单个立体摄像头的移动机器人和AR场景。从单一立体对恢复高质量3DGS仍面临遮挡、视场有限和几何缺失等挑战，亟需一种因果、高效且鲁棒的重建方法。

Method: 提出 StereoSplat：一种输入无关的前馈3D高斯估计器，能处理任意数量的带姿态立体对，融合成本体积分支与三平面3D体积分支，并采用连续姿态编码以实现泛化；引入 StereoSplat+：基于扩散模型的一次性渐进推理方案，从单个立体对出发，渲染新视图，经一步扩散增强后反馈更新3DGS，实现迭代优化。

Result: 在 KITTI-360 数据集上的实验表明，StereoSplat+ 在新视角渲染质量和几何准确性方面优于现有前馈3DGS基线，尤其在遮挡区域和强视图外推情况下表现更优。

Conclusion: StereoSplat+ 有效解决了单立体对条件下3DGS的因果重建难题，为移动设备和AR应用中的实时、高质量三维场景重建提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Recent advances in 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) have enabled high-quality, render-ready scene representations for novel-view synthesis. However, most existing 3DGS pipelines rely on multi-view observations (or non-causal access to future frames) to achieve sufficient coverage, which is often unavailable in on-device robotics and AR settings where sensing is restricted to a single stereo rig. Recovering a high-quality 3DGS scene from one stereo observation, therefore, remains challenging due to occlusions, limited field of view, and missing geometry. We present StereoSplat+, a diffusion-enhanced feed-forward framework that enables causal reconstruction from a single stereo pair. Our method builds on two key components. First, we propose StereoSplat, an input-invariant feed-forward 3D Gaussian estimator that takes a variable number of posed stereo pairs as input and predicts high-quality 3D Gaussians. StereoSplat fuses complementary geometry cues via a cost-volume branch and a triplane-based 3D volume branch and leverages continuous pose encoding to generalize across view counts and camera configurations. Second, since multiple posed stereo pairs are typically unavailable at inference time, we introduce a diffusion-enhanced one-shot progressive inference scheme called StereoSplat+: starting from one stereo pair, we render novel stereo views from the predicted 3DGS, refine them with a one-step diffusion enhancer, and feed them back as additional inputs to update the 3DGS. Experiments on the KITTI-360 dataset show that StereoSplat+ improves novel-view rendering quality and geometry accuracy, especially in occluded regions and under strong view extrapolation, outperforming recent feed-forward 3DGS baselines.

</details>


### [2] [Mixture of Probes: Learning from Privileged Modalities in Multimodal LLMs Through Probing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08839)
*Dominick Reilly,Qiyu Wu,Hiromi Wakaki,Srijan Das,Yuki Mistufuji*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出Mixture of Probes（MoP）框架，通过结构化探针机制从共享模态编码器的中间表示中提取并组织模态特定与通用信号，实现模态间信息的有效解耦。引入MoP Cross-modal Training（MoP-X）训练策略，利用探针解耦损失防止探针坍缩，促进跨模态学习。在八个任务、四种模态的全面评估中，MoP在特权模态设置下显著优于现有基线模型，相对提升高达65%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多模态大模型假设训练和推理时所有模态均可用，但现实中常出现仅训练时有辅助模态的情况。现有方法未能有效利用这些辅助模态提供的互补监督信息，因将模态视为可互换输入而非结构化信号源。因此需要一种新框架来解耦模态特异性和通用性特征，以充分利用训练阶段的额外模态信息。

Method: 提出Mixture of Probes（MoP）框架，通过结构化探针机制从共享模态编码器的中间层表示中提取模态特定与通用信号；设计MoP Cross-modal Training（MoP-X）训练策略，引入探针解耦损失以防止探针坍缩，并鼓励跨模态知识迁移。

Result: 在涵盖八项任务、四种模态的综合评估中，MoP在仅使用单一模态作为输入的推理场景下表现优异，显著超越多个强基线模型，相对性能提升最高达65%，证明了即使在推理时不可用的辅助模态，若在训练中被有效利用，仍能带来显著收益。

Conclusion: MoP框架成功实现了多模态信号的解耦与高效利用，在特权模态设置下展现出强大潜力，为多模态大模型在真实应用场景中的鲁棒性和泛化能力提供了新思路。相关代码、模型检查点及评估协议将在GitHub公开。

Abstract: Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) are typically designed under the assumption that all modalities available during training will also be accessible at inference. However, many real-world settings violate this assumption, requiring models to operate under a privileged modality setting, where auxiliary modalities are available only during training. While these modalities contain valuable information, existing MLLMs largely fail to leverage them effectively, as they treat modalities as interchangeable inputs rather than sources of complementary supervision. We propose Mixture of Probes (MoP), a novel framework that disentangles modality-specific and modality-general signals within the MLLM, allowing the model to preserve modality-dependent structure while learning transferable representations across modalities. At its core, MoP achieves this through a structured probing mechanism that extracts and organizes information from intermediate representations of a shared modality encoder, rather than relying only on final-layer alignment as done in existing MLLMs. To support this disentanglement, we further introduce MoP Cross-modal Training (MoP-X), a training strategy for MoP centered around a probe disentanglement loss that prevents probe collapse and encourages cross-modal learning. We evaluate MoP across two domains spanning eight tasks and four modalities under a comprehensive evaluation protocol tailored to the privileged modality setting, where each modality is independently treated as the sole input at inference time. MoP consistently outperforms strong MLLM baselines, achieving up to 65% relative improvement, demonstrating that auxiliary modalities, even when unavailable at inference, can provide substantial gains when effectively leveraged during training. Code, model checkpoints, and evaluation protocols will be made available at https://github.com/Sony/MoP.

</details>


### [3] [Secure-by-Disguise: A Systematic Evaluation of Image Disguising for Confidential Medical Image Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08867)
*Jason Rojas,Jiajie He,Yash Patel,Yuechun Gu,Zeyun Yu,Keke Chen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该研究评估了两种主流的图像伪装技术（DisguisedNets和NeuraCrypt）在医疗图像分类与语义分割任务中的隐私保护与模型性能表现。结果显示，伪装技术在分类任务中保持了较好的预测效用，但在密集型分割任务中导致显著性能下降；其中随机多维变换（RMT）在性能与安全性间取得最佳平衡，而基于AES的伪装方法严重损害了模型效用。此外，针对自然图像有效的基于回归的重建攻击在真实医疗图像上效果较差。整体表明，图像伪装技术在医疗AI应用中具有潜力，但需根据任务类型谨慎选择。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决云环境下医疗图像深度学习带来的隐私泄露问题，探索图像伪装作为隐私增强技术的有效性与适用性。

Method: 建立统一评估框架，对DisguisedNets和NeuraCrypt两种图像伪装方法在四个数据集上的分类与语义分割任务中进行性能、效率与抗重建攻击能力的系统评估。

Result: 图像伪装在医学图像分类中保留了良好效用，但在语义分割中造成显著性能下降；RMT表现最优，AES伪装严重损害模型性能；基于回归的重建攻击在真实医疗图像上效果有限。

Conclusion: 图像伪装技术可为保密医疗人工智能提供有效支持，但其适用性依赖于具体任务类型，需权衡性能与安全，未来应针对医疗图像特性优化伪装方法。

Abstract: Cloud-based deep learning enables large-scale medical image analysis but raises significant privacy concerns when sensitive patient images are outsourced for model development. Image disguising has recently emerged as a promising privacy-enhancing technology (PET) that transforms images into visually unintelligible representations while preserving information for downstream learning. We established a unified framework to evaluate representative methods, DisguisedNets and NeuraCrypt, across four datasets involving classification and semantic segmentation tasks. Our analysis assessed predictive utility, efficiency, and robustness against reconstruction attacks. Results showed that image disguising performance varies significantly between tasks; while methods preserved utility for medical image classification, they caused substantial degradation in dense semantic segmentation. Specifically, Randomized Multidimensional Transformation (RMT) offered the optimal balance of performance and security, whereas AES-based disguising severely impacted utility. Furthermore, regression-based reconstruction attacks effective on natural images proved considerably less successful on realistic medical images. These findings provide a systematic assessment of PET suitability for confidential medical AI applications.

</details>


### [4] [Decoupled Illumination Priors for Spatially Controllable Multi-View Indoor Scene Relighting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08879)
*Chenjian Gao,Linning Xu,Tianfan Xue*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Lume-Palette 是一种用于室内场景重光照的渐进式框架，通过解耦光照提取与光照投射两阶段，实现语义光照先验下的空间可控多视角重光照。该方法利用预训练扩散模型提取标准光照调色板以保持材质-光照交互的真实性，并通过粗略3D几何信息显式映射目标空间光照条件。为高效处理密集多视角和多模态输入，引入非对称多视角条件策略，选择性注入关键空间上下文。实验表明，该方法在合成与真实场景中均能生成逼真、空间可控且多视角一致的重光照结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 室内场景重光照需要高度逼真、精确的空间控制以及严格的多视角一致性。现有基于扩散模型的图像编辑方法虽可通过文本提示实现语义光照操作，但难以精确控制3D光源位置，常破坏其生成先验。因此，亟需一种既能保持真实材质-光照交互，又能实现空间精准控制的重光照方法。

Method: 提出Lume-Palette框架，分为两个阶段：(1) 光照蒸馏阶段，从预训练扩散模型中提取标准化的光照调色板，保留真实的材料-光照相互作用；(2) 光照投射阶段，基于粗略3D几何信息显式映射目标空间光照条件。采用非对称多视角条件策略，仅选择性注入必要的空间上下文信息，提升效率与一致性。

Result: 在多种合成与真实场景上验证，Lume-Palette能够生成高保真的多视角一致重光照结果，具备良好的空间可控性与视觉真实性，显著优于现有方法。

Conclusion: Lume-Palette通过解耦光照建模与空间控制，有效结合了扩散模型的生成能力与3D几何引导的精确性，实现了高质量、可控且一致的室内场景重光照，为复杂光照编辑提供了新范式。

Abstract: Indoor scene relighting demands photorealism, precise spatial control, and strict multi-view consistency. While diffusion-based image editing models enable semantic lighting manipulation via text prompts, enforcing exact 3D light placement often disrupts their generative priors. We propose Lume-Palette, a progressive framework that leverages semantic lighting priors for spatially controllable multi-view indoor relighting. The approach decouples relighting into two stages: (1) illumination distillation, which extracts canonical illumination palettes from a pretrained diffusion model to preserve realistic material-light interactions, and (2) illumination casting, which explicitly maps target spatial lighting conditions defined from coarse 3D geometry. To efficiently handle dense multi-view and multi-modal inputs, we introduce an asymmetric multi-view conditioning strategy that selectively injects essential spatial context. Experiments on diverse synthetic scenes and real-world scenes demonstrate that Lume-Palette produces photorealistic, spatially controllable, and multi-view consistent relighting results. Project Page: https://cjeen.github.io/lumepalette

</details>


### [5] [HAT Super-Resolution and a PARSeq+CLIP4STR Voting Ensemble for Extreme In-the-Wild License Plate Recognition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08896)
*Karthik Sivarama Krishnan,Koushik Sivarama Krishnan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本论文提出了一种用于极端野外车牌超分辨率（XLPSR）的系统，结合了混合注意力变压器（HAT）前端与双场景文本识别器（PARSeq-S和CLIP4STR-B），并通过置信度加权字符投票机制在不确定位置进行回避。该方法将XLPSR视为一个由图像可读性控制的识别任务，利用非对称评分规则（+2 / -1 / 0）通过弃权策略优化性能。系统在RTX 3090上每序列平均耗时1.7秒，远低于60秒的时限要求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决极端野外条件下车牌图像质量极低导致的识别困难问题，通过超分辨率重建提升字符可读性，并利用非对称评分规则优化识别准确率。

Method: 采用混合注意力变压器（HAT）进行图像超分辨率重建，结合两个场景文本识别模型（PARSeq-S和CLIP4STR-B）的集成，并引入置信度加权字符投票机制，在识别不确定性高的位置主动放弃输出，以减少错误。

Result: 在公开验证集上获得9.73的wECR得分，系统处理速度为1.7秒/序列（最坏情况2.7秒，99%分位数2.4秒），满足60秒/序列的计算预算限制。

Conclusion: 所提出的系统有效融合了超分辨率与文本识别技术，通过智能弃权策略应对极端复杂场景下的识别挑战，具备高精度与实时性，适用于实际部署。

Abstract: We describe our entry to the ICIP 2026 Grand Challenge on Extreme In-the-Wild License Plate Super-Resolution (XLPSR), which scored 9.73 wECR on the public validation leaderboard. The system pairs a Hybrid Attention Transformer super-resolution (HAT) front-end with an ensemble of two scene-text recognisers (PARSeq-S and CLIP4STR-B) and a confidence-weighted character-voting scheme that abstains on uncertain positions. We treat XLPSR as a recognition task gated by image legibility: the SR step exists to lift characters out of sub-pixel territory, and the asymmetric scoring rule (+2 / -1 / 0) is exploited explicitly through abstention. Our pipeline runs in 1.7 s per sequence on RTX 3090 (max 2.7 s, p99 2.4 s), well under the 60 s/sequence Docker budget.

</details>


### [6] [Vision Transformers Learn Gestalt-Like Figure-Ground Cues from Natural Images](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08932)
*Matthias Tangemann,Benjamin Lo,Zygmunt Pizlo,Kaleem Siddiqi,Dirk B. Walther,Sven Dickinson*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本研究评估了视觉变压器（ViTs）在形状基础的图形-背景组织中的表现，通过自然图像和人工控制刺激测试25个不同训练目标的ViTs，发现其能稳健编码包围性和凸性，且在自然图像上训练的线性探测器可零样本泛化到人工刺激；对称性则仅在均匀着色区域被编码，而在纹理区域表现不佳。结果表明，格式塔式图形-背景线索可从自然场景统计中学习，并使ViTs成为研究感知组织计算机制的理想模型系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解形状基础的图形-背景组织如何在自然条件下运作，以及这些线索如何从自然场景的统计特性中产生，是当前视觉感知研究的重要问题。现有研究多基于抽象刺激，缺乏对真实世界条件下的探索。深度神经网络尤其是视觉变压器（ViTs）提供了模拟人类视觉系统潜在机制的可能性，因此需要评估其是否能够学习并表征这些关键的形状线索。

Method: 使用25个涵盖监督与自监督训练目标的视觉变压器（ViTs），通过在线性探测器中拟合中间补丁表示来预测图形-背景分配，分别在自然图像和隔离单一线索的人工刺激上进行测试。采用零样本泛化能力评估模型对未见刺激的适应性，并分析各形状线索（包围性、凸性、对称性）的编码情况。

Result: ViTs在自然图像上训练后，表现出对包围性和凸性的稳健编码，且线性探测器具有良好的零样本泛化能力，能有效预测人工刺激中的图形-背景划分。对于对称性，模型仅在均匀颜色区域有效编码，在纹理区域表现不佳，表明其对对称性的感知依赖于视觉上下文。

Conclusion: 形状基础的图形-背景组织线索（如包围性、凸性、对称性）可通过自然场景的统计规律在深度神经网络中学习获得。视觉变压器展现出与人类相似的感知组织能力，具备作为研究感知组织计算机制的可靠模型系统的潜力。

Abstract: Figure-ground organization in the human visual system relies on several shape-based cues, including surroundedness, convexity, and symmetry. While these cues have been extensively studied using abstract stimuli, little is known about how they operate under natural conditions or how they arise from the statistics of natural scenes. Deep neural networks offer a promising path forward: a model that relies on the same figure-ground cues as humans would provide tractable experimental access to the underlying mechanisms. In this study, we evaluate shape-based figure-ground organization in Vision Transformers (ViTs), for which prior work has demonstrated the emergence of object-based grouping. We test 25 ViTs spanning supervised and self-supervised training objectives, by fitting linear probes to predict figure-ground assignment from intermediate patch representations using both natural images and controlled artificial stimuli that isolate individual cues. Our results show that ViTs robustly encode surroundedness and convexity, and that probes trained on natural images generalize zero-shot to artificial stimuli across several models. For symmetry we observe mixed results: the cue is encoded for uniformly colored but not for textured regions. Taken together, our findings demonstrate that Gestalt-like figure-ground cues can be learned from natural scene statistics and position ViTs as a compelling model system for studying the computational mechanisms of perceptual organization.
  Code and data is available at https://github.com/mtangemann/mlvbench

</details>


### [7] [Is sub-metre resolution necessary for cocoa mapping? A landscape-stratified evaluation of very high resolution imagery, decametric Earth Observation inputs, and operational products in Cote d'Ivoire](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08945)
*Kasimir Orlowski,Filip Sabo,Michele Meroni,Astrid Verhegghen,Mariana Belgiu,Felix Rembold*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本研究评估了在科特迪瓦不同景观条件下，使用超高分辨率（VHR）影像、中分辨率遥感影像及基础模型嵌入进行可可树地图绘制的性能差异。结果表明，VHR模型表现最佳（F1=0.92），在所有景观梯度下均保持稳定；基于TESSERA的基础模型表现优于AEF和Sentinel-2，而现有公开产品中以Kalischek产品表现最好（F1=0.83）。在破碎化程度高或树冠密度极端的区域，VHR与中分辨率方法的性能差距扩大，说明针对复杂可可种植区采用定向VHR采集具有显著优势，而基础模型嵌入则为大范围制图提供了可扩展的替代方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准确的可可种植地图对森林砍伐监测、供应链透明度和监管应用日益重要。传统中分辨率遥感影像在小农混合型景观中因空间聚合问题可能限制可可识别精度，因此需要评估不同影像分辨率和模型方法在复杂景观中的表现差异。

Method: 利用0.5米Pleiades VHR影像、10米Sentinel-2年度合成影像以及TESSERA和AlphaEarth Foundation（AEF）基础模型的嵌入特征，构建可可地图模型，并对比4个公开可可地图产品。通过2,821个独立判读的参考点，在树冠密度和景观破碎化梯度上进行分层精度评估。

Result: VHR模型达到最高性能（F1=0.92），且在所有景观分层中保持F1值高于0.90；在十米级输入中，TESSERA表现最优（F1=0.86），其次为AEF（F1=0.82）和Sentinel-2（F1=0.76）；公开产品中Kalischek产品表现最好（F1=0.83），与内部训练的AEF模型相当。在高破碎化或极端树冠密度条件下，VHR与十米级方法的性能差距增大。

Conclusion: 在复杂可可种植景观中，定向获取超高分辨率影像可显著提升地图精度，尤其适用于破碎化严重或树冠覆盖极端的区域；而基础模型嵌入提供了一种可扩展的大范围制图解决方案，可在资源有限时作为有效替代。

Abstract: Accurate cocoa mapping is increasingly important for deforestation monitoring, supply-chain transparency, and regulatory applications. Spatial aggregation in conventional medium-resolution Earth observation (EO) imagery may limit cocoa detection in heterogeneous smallholder landscapes. In Cote d'Ivoire, we therefore evaluated how mapping performance varies across landscape conditions, whether very high resolution (VHR) imagery provides a meaningful advantage, and whether foundation-model embeddings improve decametric cocoa mapping. We developed models using 0.5 m Pleiades VHR imagery, a 10 m Sentinel-2 annual composite, and embeddings from TESSERA and AlphaEarth Foundations (AEF), and additionally assessed four publicly available cocoa mapping products. Performance was evaluated through a landscape-stratified accuracy assessment using 2,821 independently interpreted reference points distributed across gradients of tree cover density and landscape fragmentation. The VHR model achieved the highest performance (F1 = 0.92) and maintained F1-scores above 0.90 across all strata. Among the decametric inputs, TESSERA performed best (F1 = 0.86), followed by AEF (F1 = 0.82) and Sentinel-2 (F1 = 0.76). Of the existing cocoa products, the Kalischek product performed best (F1 = 0.83), comparable to the internally trained AEF model. Performance differences between VHR and decametric approaches increased with fragmentation and under low and high tree cover density conditions. Targeted VHR acquisition may therefore be particularly beneficial in complex cocoa landscapes, while foundation-model embeddings offer a scalable alternative for large-area mapping.

</details>


### [8] [MultiView-Bench: A Diagnostic Benchmark for World-Centric Multi-View Integration in VLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08970)
*Hantao Zhang,Jinru Sui,Ed Li,Dirk Bergemann,Zhuoran Yang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出MultiView-Bench基准，评估视觉语言模型在多视角整合与3D场景理解方面的能力，发现现有模型在3D空间关系和跨视图信息融合上表现不佳，并提出ViewNavigator多智能体框架以提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉语言模型评估多集中于单视角或有限视角感知，缺乏对多视角整合以构建全局3D认知模型的能力测试，而这一能力对机械部件组装等下游任务至关重要。

Method: 设计MultiView-Bench基准，要求模型将物体位置从相机视角中解耦并定位到固定全局坐标系；采用多智能体框架ViewNavigator，主动选择信息丰富的视角，进行感知与多视图信息融合。

Result: 前沿视觉语言模型在2D平面关系上表现良好，但在3D空间关系和跨视图信息整合上存在显著缺陷；ViewNavigator在预算匹配条件下显著提升基线模型性能，全量版本提升3-5倍。

Conclusion: 当前VLMs在构建世界中心的3D认知模型方面仍存在根本性局限，需通过主动感知与多视角融合机制加以改进，MultiView-Bench为评估此类能力提供了有效工具。

Abstract: Recent benchmarks for VLMs largely assess single- or limited-view perception, leaving untested the core cognitive ability to integrate observations across viewpoints into a coherent, world-centric (allocentric) 3D mental model. We introduce MultiView-Bench, a diagnostic benchmark expressly designed to evaluate multi-view integration for holistic 3D scene comprehension. Unlike existing datasets that focus on pixel-level mapping or camera-relative navigation, MultiView-Bench requires models to decouple object positioning from transient perspectives and ground them in a fixed global coordinate system. This capability serves as a prerequisite for VLMs before being deployed for downstream tasks such as mechanical part assembly. Our systematic evaluation of frontier VLMs reveals consistent failure modes: strong performance on 2D planar relations from a single image, but marked difficulty with 3D spatial relations and with aggregating information across views. We further identify biases in VLMs, such as struggles with unconventional axis directions and sensitivity to object colorways and texture variations. Acknowledging these limitations, we propose ViewNavigator, a multi-agent framework that actively selects informative viewpoints, perceives, and fuses multi-view evidence, improving diverse base models on MultiView-Bench even under a strict budget-matched comparison (and by 3-5x for the full agent).

### [9] [C-GAP: Class-Aware and Online Prompting Improves Vision-Language Models on Imbalanced Classes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09008)
*Francis Fernandez,Arash Jahangiri,Salimeh Sekeh*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: C-GAP是一种检测器无关、无需标注的框架，通过迭代优化语言提示来提升少数类检测性能。它分为两阶段：首先构建结合场景描述与类别数量上下文的复合标题基线；其次利用大语言模型对每张图像的标题进行迭代精炼，基于动态阈值判断是否接受、暂存或重新生成，直至达到足够性能提升。整个过程不更新检测器权重。实验表明，C-GAP在少数类AP@0.5上相比基线最高提升53%，在COCO上相对提升约81%（17.69 → 32.09），验证了复合标题作为精炼基础的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 安全关键感知系统需可靠检测小标签空间中的稀有目标类别，而现有长尾检测方法针对数百个密集标注类别设计，无法解决此问题。开放词汇检测虽可通过自然语言查询提升性能，但其效果依赖提示质量，因此提出通过迭代优化提示来缓解类别不平衡问题，避免重训练或额外标注。

Method: 提出C-GAP（Caption-Guided Augmentation and Prompting）框架，分两阶段：1）构建复合标题基线，融合图像场景描述与类别数量上下文；2）使用大语言模型对每张图像的标题进行个体化迭代精炼，根据少数类AP@0.5与动态阈值比较，决定是否接受、暂存或重生成，直至满足性能增益条件。全程冻结检测器权重，无参数更新。

Result: C-GAP显著提升少数类平均精度，在多个开放词汇架构和基准上表现优越；在COCO数据集上，少数类AP@0.5从17.69提升至32.09，相对提升约81%；若以仅场景描述或仅类别数量提示为起点，则改进效果有限，说明复合标题是有效精炼的基础。

Conclusion: C-GAP证明了通过迭代优化语言提示可有效缓解少数类检测中的类别不平衡问题，且复合标题基线与迭代精炼两阶段缺一不可，为开放词汇检测提供了一种高效、无需标注的性能增强新范式。

Abstract: Safety-critical perception systems must reliably detect rare object classes within small label spaces, a setting that long-tailed detection methods, designed for hundreds of classes with dense annotation, fundamentally do not address. Open-vocabulary detectors offer a promising alternative, as they use natural language queries at inference time, making prompt quality a first-class lever for detection performance. We exploit this property to address class imbalance: rather than retraining models or collecting additional annotations, we ask whether iteratively refining the language prompts, fed to frozen detectors, can improve minority class detection. We introduce C-GAP Caption-Guided Augmentation and Prompting), a detector-agnostic, annotation-free framework that operates in two phases. First, we establish a composite caption baseline combining per-image scene descriptions with class-quantity context, which we show outperforms scene-description only or class-quantity-only prompts across multiple open-vocabulary architectures and benchmarks. Second, an LLM iteratively refines each image's caption individually, with trials triaged into accept, tentative, or regenerate buckets based on minority-class AP@0.5 against a dynamic threshold derived from the composite baseline. Refinement terminates early once sufficient AP@0.5 gain is achieved. No detector weights are updated at any stage. Our experiments shows that C-GAP improves minority-class average precision up to 53% over the baselines. On COCO, C-GAP improves minority-class AP@0.5 by ~81% relative over the composite baseline (17.69 -> 32.09). Experiments confirm that composite captions provide the critical foundation for effective refinement: using scene-description-only or class-quantity-only prompts as the refinement starting point yields diminishing returns, supporting both stages of C-GAP as necessary contributions.

Method: 提出GenCeption模型，基于预训练的视频生成扩散模型构建前馈感知架构，通过文本指令驱动完成多样化视觉任务，实现端到端的通用视觉理解。

Conclusion: 视频生成不仅是一种内容合成手段，更是一种推动通用视觉智能发展的基础范式，为实现面向物理世界的通用视觉模型提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Driven by next-token prediction, NLP shifted from task-specific models into powerful generalist foundation models. What, then, is the equivalent catalyst needed to achieve a general-purpose model in computer vision? In this paper, we contend that large-scale text-to-video generation serves as a strong pre-training paradigm for computer vision, providing the necessary spatiotemporal priors, vision-language alignment, and scalability required for general visual intelligence. We introduce GenCeption, which leverages a pre-trained video generative diffusion backbone to define a feed-forward perception model, capable of performing various vision tasks steered by text instructions. Empirical results demonstrate that GenCeption achieves state-of-the-art performance across a diverse suite of tasks, including depth, surface normal, and camera pose estimation, expression-referring segmentation, and 3D keypoint prediction, often matching or surpassing specialized models (e.g. DepthAnything3, SAM3, D4RT, VGGT-Omega, Sapiens, David, Genmo, and Lotus-2). Furthermore, the video generative pretrained backbone outperforms alternative pretraining paradigms (e.g., V-JEPA, and Video MAE) under comparable settings. Importantly, GenCeption exhibits preliminary data and model scaling properties along with exceptional data efficiency, where it achieves comparable performance with leading models like D4RT and VGGT-Omega with 7 to 500 less training data. Finally, GenCeption also exhibits intriguing emergent behaviors: a model trained exclusively on synthetic human videos generalizes to real-world footage and out-of-distribution object categories (e.g., animals and robots). These findings suggest that video generation is not merely a synthesis tool, but a foundational path toward generalist vision intelligence for the physical world. Project page: https://genception.github.io

### [11] [MOSAIC: Adaptive Inter-layer Composition for Efficient Heterogeneous Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09029)
*Yuncheng Yang,Feiyang Ye,Shixian Luo,Yinna Zhu,Lianlei Shan,Wangcai Zhao,Kuo Zhang,Yan Chen,Yong Wu,Yan Xie*

TL;DR: MOSAIC提出一种硬件感知的自动搜索方法，将同质化视觉语言模型转化为异构优化架构，通过多目标混合整数规划选择高效算子（如线性、稀疏、低秩），在保证性能的同时显著降低推理延迟。引入两阶段参数恢复机制以缓解结构变换带来的性能下降，最终实现仅需不到2%训练成本即达到基线性能，并带来1.76倍预填充和2.54倍解码加速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有异构架构依赖手工设计的静态混合模式，难以适应不同硬件且效率不优。需要一种可自动适配硬件的优化方法来提升视觉语言模型的推理效率与性能平衡。

Method: 提出MOSAIC方法，构建包含多种高效算子的统一搜索空间，将配置选择建模为多目标混合整数规划问题，并采用两阶段参数恢复策略：全局离策略蒸馏稳定内部表征，双教师在线策略蒸馏结合大模型知识扩展与原模型分布稳定性。

Result: MOSAIC-4B在多个基准测试中表现与原始4B模型相当，训练成本低于2%，推理速度提升1.76倍（预填充）和2.54倍（解码）。

Conclusion: MOSAIC实现了对视觉语言模型的高效、自适应异构结构优化，在保持高性能的同时大幅降低训练开销与推理延迟，具备强实用性和可扩展性。

Abstract: Vision-Language Models (VLMs) have achieved success using homogeneous Transformers to process multimedia data. Recent studies show that heterogeneous structures interleaving efficient mechanisms, like linear attention, improve both performance and inference latency over homogeneous designs. However, these efforts rely on handcrafted static mixing patterns, which are sub-optimal and difficult to adapt to specific hardware. To bridge this gap, we propose Multi-Objective Search for Adaptive Inter-layer Composition (MOSAIC), a hardware-aware search method that automatically transforms homogeneous models into optimized heterogeneous architectures. MOSAIC integrates diverse efficiency mechanisms--including linear, sparse, and low-rank operators--into a unified search space. By formulating the selection as a multi-objective Mixed Integer Programming (MIP) problem, our method identifies optimal configurations that maximize downstream performance under strict hardware latency constraints. To mitigate performance degradation from structural transitions, we introduce a two-stage parameter recovery process: global off-policy distillation to stabilize internal representations, followed by a dual-teacher on-policy distillation leveraging a 235B oracle for knowledge expansion and the original 4B teacher for distributional stability. We validate MOSAIC through MOSAIC-4B, derived from Qwen3-VL-4B-Instruct. Results demonstrate that MOSAIC-4B matches the baseline's performance across multiple benchmarks while requiring less than 2% of the original training cost. Furthermore, it substantially improves inference efficiency, achieving 1.76x prefilling and 2.54x decoding speedups.

In contrast, existing unsupervised approaches typically depend on generative models or clustering-based stage-wise optimization, which are prone to distribution bias and the accumulation of noisy pseudo-labels. To address these limitations, we propose STEAM (Stable Self-Training with Elastic Matching and Adaptive Purification), an end-to-end unsupervised cross-view geo-localization framework that performs self-training directly on real drone and satellite images. Specifically, the proposed Stable Spatial-Aware Module enhances the stability of feature representations, Elastic Matching discovers high-quality cross-view pseudo-labels, and Adaptive Purification dynamically maintains a reliable pseudo-label repository throughout the self-training process. Extensive experiments on the University-1652 and SUES-200 benchmarks demonstrate that STEAM achieves state-of-the-art performance among all existing unsupervised methods and delivers performance comparable to supervised approaches, validating the effectiveness and superiority of the proposed framework. The source code is available at https://github.com/wsx-heu/STEAM.git.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: A striking feature of the human visual system is that it ingests visual information through a series of local foveated glimpses, rather than a single global computation. This makes human vision distinctly different from most popular computer vision models in use today, which input images globally and in a single shot. A natural question therefore is whether local, sequential vision models may provide any fundamental computational benefits in addition to being biologically more plausible than global models. In this work, we investigate this question from the perspective of visual state tracking and length generalization. Inspired by recent studies of length generalization in language models, we study the behavior of vision models trained on simple vision tasks that require the aggregation of local information across an image. Our experiments reveal that, similar to language models, vision models can learn to exploit global shortcuts and thereby fail to generalize over task length or complexity. We also show that recurrent vision policies based on strictly local perception can mitigate these failures, thereby allowing models to generalize on these tasks. Our results show that local attention may be an essential overlooked requirement for robust compositional generalization.

### [14] [Probing Diffusion Denoising Dynamics for Contrastive Representation Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09067)
*Yasong Dai,Zeeshan Hayder,David Ahmedt-Aristizabal,Hongdong Li*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出D$^3$CL框架，通过利用扩散模型不同噪声时间步的随机视图，结合对比学习与去噪重建损失，实现参数高效的判别性表征学习，保持生成能力。在ImageNet-1K上达到80.1%线性探测准确率，生成FID为5.56。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索如何在不破坏生成能力的前提下，通过轻量级更新适配预训练扩散模型以支持判别性表征学习。

Method: 利用不同扩散时间步的噪声潜在表示作为同一图像的随机视图，设计对比学习目标，并结合标准去噪重建损失；采用LoRA对Stable Diffusion骨干网络进行参数高效更新，冻结原模型参数。

Result: 在ImageNet-1K上实现80.1%线性探测准确率和256×256无条件生成下5.56的FID值；消融实验表明采样位置与方式影响扩散特征有效性。

Conclusion: D$^3$CL证明了重建与噪声级别对比目标的互补性，是一种参数高效且能同时提升判别性能与生成质量的扩散模型适应框架。

Abstract: Text-to-image diffusion models exhibit unprecedented generative capability and contain rich intermediate representations that can be useful for discriminative vision tasks. Motivated by this observation, we study a focused question: how can the denoising dynamics of a pretrained diffusion model be adapted to support discriminative representation learning while preserving its generative behavior under parameter-efficient updates? We present D$^3$CL as an investigation of this question. Our key observation is that noisy latents at different diffusion timesteps can be interpreted as stochastic views of the same underlying image, enabling a contrastive objective to be coupled with the standard denoising reconstruction loss. This formulation provides a simple way to probe the interaction between generative denoising and discriminative representation learning without training from scratch. To keep the adaptation lightweight, we apply LoRA updates to a pretrained Stable Diffusion backbone while freezing the original model parameters. D$^3$CL provides strong empirical evidence that reconstruction and noise-level contrastive objectives can be complementary: on ImageNet-1K, it obtains 80.1% linear-probing accuracy and an FID of 5.56 for $256 \times 256$ unconditional generation. Additional ablations on the design space suggest that the usefulness of diffusion features depends on where and how denoising states are sampled. These results establish D$^3$CL as a parameter-efficient adaptation framework for pretrained diffusion models, showing that noise-level contrastive learning can structure denoising representations for discriminative tasks while maintaining generative performance.

### [15] [OmniMapBench: Benchmarking Visual-Centric Reasoning on Diverse Map Documents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09068)

TL;DR: OmniMapBench introduces a new benchmark for visually grounded reasoning in map documents, addressing the limitation of existing benchmarks that rely too heavily on text. It features 2,096 QA pairs across 1,603 maps from nine categories, designed to assess a range of visual reasoning skills. The Visual Dependency Index (VDI) measures how much performance drops when images are replaced with text descriptions, showing OmniMapBench requires genuine visual understanding. Evaluations on 25 LVLMs reveal a top accuracy of only 75.03%, highlighting significant challenges. The dataset and code are publicly available.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing document understanding benchmarks often allow high performance without true visual grounding, as visual content can be reduced to text. This undermines the evaluation of genuine visual reasoning capabilities in LVLMs. To address this, a new benchmark focused on irreducible visual reasoning is needed.

Method: OmniMapBench is constructed with 2,096 manually annotated QA pairs across 1,603 map documents spanning nine categories. A hierarchy of reasoning skills is incorporated, from basic perception to complex multi-step visual reasoning. The Visual Dependency Index (VDI) is introduced to measure the necessity of visual input by comparing model performance with actual images versus question-agnostic image descriptions.

Result: OmniMapBench shows a significantly higher VDI than existing benchmarks, confirming its emphasis on irreducible visual reasoning. Evaluation of 25 leading LVLMs reveals a substantial performance gap, with the best model achieving only 75.03% accuracy, indicating current models struggle with advanced visual-centric tasks.

Conclusion: OmniMapBench effectively advances the evaluation of visual-centric reasoning in LVLMs by focusing on truly visual tasks. It provides a challenging benchmark that exposes limitations in current models and aims to drive future research in robust document understanding.

Abstract: Recent advancements in LVLMs necessitate robust benchmarks for complex, visually grounded reasoning. A critical limitation is identified in many document understanding benchmarks: visual content is often reducible to text, enabling high performance without genuine visual grounding. To address this limitation, OmniMapBench is introduced to foster visual-centric reasoning for map documents. The benchmark comprises 2,096 manually annotated question-answer pairs across 1,603 map documents from nine categories. It is designed to probe a hierarchy of skills, ranging from perception to multi-step visual reasoning. To quantify benchmark properties, a simple yet effective benchmark-level metric is proposed: the Visual Dependency Index (VDI), defined as the accuracy drop when images are replaced with question-agnostic descriptions. OmniMapBench exhibits higher VDI than established benchmarks, which quantitatively validates its focus on irreducible visual reasoning. Comprehensive evaluations of 25 leading LVLMs are conducted on OmniMapBench. A significant performance gap is observed, with the top-performing model achieving only 75.03\% accuracy. This result underscores the challenges posed by OmniMapBench to current LVLMs. This work aims to catalyze progress in visual-centric reasoning for document understanding of LVLMs. The dataset and code are publicly available at https://github.com/SIGMME/OmniMapBench.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视频令牌压缩方法依赖帧级显著性或启发式令牌合并，容易过度关注局部显著区域并产生模糊融合特征，限制了视频大模型的效率。

Method: 引入上下文最远点锚定（CFPA）以保留显著、一致且高覆盖的骨架令牌；采用轨迹约束残差凝聚（TCRC）通过一对一时间轨迹和受约束的近流形凝聚压缩残差令牌，生成可追溯的事件令牌。

Result: 在四个视频理解基准上评估，使用仅10%的视觉令牌，LLaVA-OneVision实现了12.99倍的TFLOPs降低，同时保持99.1%的原始性能，证明了方法的有效性和泛化能力。

Conclusion: GeoTrace提供了一种紧凑且可追溯的令牌表示，显著提升了视频大模型推理的效率与鲁棒性。

Abstract: Although Video Large Language Models (Video LLMs) have shown strong performance in video understanding, their efficiency is still limited by the large number of visual tokens. Existing video token compression methods typically rely on frame-wise saliency or heuristic token merging, which can over-focus on locally salient regions and produce ambiguous fused features. To address these issues, we propose GeoTrace, a training-free spatiotemporal token compression framework that decomposes video evidence into exact skeleton tokens and traceable residual event tokens. Specifically, Contextual Farthest-Point Anchoring (CFPA) preserves salient, context-consistent, and high-coverage skeleton tokens, while Trajectory-Constrained Residual Condensation (TCRC) compresses residual tokens through one-to-one temporal trajectories and constrained near-manifold condensation, producing traceable event tokens with reduced ambiguity. We evaluate GeoTrace on four Video LLMs across four video understanding benchmarks, and the results demonstrate its effectiveness and generalization across different model architectures and scenarios. On LLaVA-OneVision, with only 10\% visual tokens retained, GeoTrace achieves a \(12.99\times\) TFLOPs reduction while preserving 99.1\% of the vanilla performance. Overall, GeoTrace offers a compact and traceable token representation for efficient and robust Video LLM inference. Code is available at \href{https://github.com/guohuan-xie/GeoTrace.git}{\texttt{Code}}.

### [18] [Adaptive Latent Trajectory Anchoring for Action Segmentation Dataset Condensation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09081)

Abstract: Dataset condensation for action segmentation synthesizes compact, informative representations of long, untrimmed video datasets. The existing approach relies on Variational Autoencoders and an iterative latent optimization; it is computationally expensive and suffers from over-smoothed reconstructions and rigid temporal constraints. This paper proposes to shift the condensation paradigm from optimization-based inversion to deterministic latent mapping. By leveraging Denoising Diffusion Implicit Models, we represent action segments as continuous trajectories anchored by sparse latent points in the noise manifold. To maximize representational efficiency, we introduce an adaptive allocation mechanism that dynamically redistributes the anchoring budget based on segment-wise reconstruction difficulty. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our framework significantly outperforms state-of-the-art methods in segmentation performance across common datasets. Notably, our approach achieves performance parity with real data training while maintaining a condensation ratio of 2.4\% on Breakfast dataset.

### [19] [REBASE: Reference-Background Subspace Elimination for Training-Free In-Context Segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09082)
*Mantha Sai Gopal,Jaison Saji Chacko,Harsh Nandwana,Sandesh Hegde,Debarshi Banerjee,Uma Mahesh*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: REBASE 是一种无需训练的框架，通过显式抑制参考图像与查询图像之间的虚假上下文对应关系，提升单样本分割的性能。它利用参考图像提取低秩背景特征子空间，并将参考和查询特征投影到其正交补空间中，从而获得更清晰的语义匹配。结合相似性加权的远点采样生成正向点提示，配合优化的密集相似性先验，实现了无需训练的最新性能，在 PACO-Part、FSS-1000 及跨域数据集 ISIC2018 上表现优异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有训练-free 方法受限于跨图像相似性图的质量，参考与查询图像间的共享背景导致非目标区域相似性误增，影响提示定位精度。为解决此问题，需显式消除虚假背景对应关系。

Method: 从参考图像中识别低秩背景特征子空间，将参考与查询特征投影至其正交补空间（闭式解），实现背景抑制；采用相似性加权的远点采样生成正向点提示，并引入精细的密集相似性先验以增强定位能力。

Result: 在 PACO-Part、FSS-1000 和 ISIC2018 等多个数据集上，无需任何训练或参数更新，显著超越现有训练-free 方法，达到新基准性能。

Conclusion: 显式移除背景特征子空间是提升单样本定位性能的有效原则，REBASE 证明了该方法在训练-free 分割中的强大潜力。

Abstract: Training-free in-context segmentation enables new object categories to be introduced at inference time from a single annotated reference image, eliminating the retraining and memory overhead of class-incremental learning. Recent approaches achieve this by combining vision foundation models for semantic correspondence with promptable segmentation networks like SAM. However, their performance is fundamentally limited by the quality of the cross-image similarity map; shared contextual backgrounds between the reference and query systematically elevate similarity in non-target regions, degrading prompt localization. We present REBASE, a training-free framework that explicitly suppresses these spurious contextual correspondences. Our method identifies the low-rank background feature subspace from the reference image and project the reference and query features onto its orthogonal complement in closed form, yielding cleaner semantic matching. We then generate positive point prompts using similarity-weighted farthest-point sampling, paired with a refined dense similarity prior. Without any training or parameter updates, our approach establishes a new state of the art among training-free methods on PACO-Part, FSS-1000, and cross-domain datasets such as ISIC2018, demonstrating that explicit background subspace removal is a highly effective principle for one-shot localization.

### [20] [Subtoken Vision Transformer for Fine-grained Recognition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09086)
*Jie Zhu,Ivy Zhang,Minchul Kim,Xiaoming Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: SubViT是一种用于细粒度视觉识别的选择性图像标记化方法，通过在关键区域使用多个子标记来增强局部细节表达，同时保持全局上下文。采用两阶段训练策略：第一阶段利用随机注意力头采样的分割区域微调ViT，第二阶段通过特征退化距离识别重要注意力图，并将其压缩为轻量级单图路由器以预测确定性的标记重要性分数。在GCD任务上，SubViT将DINOv2的平均新类别准确率从81.3%提升至84.7%，仅增加0.50毫秒延迟和3.4%计算量，且相比Retina Patch降低73.8%延迟。在CIFAR-10和ImageNet-100上也表现出良好泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准Vision Transformer将每个固定大小的图像块压缩为单一标记，但细粒度区分往往依赖于少数区域内的局部差异，现有方法未能有效分配额外容量到关键区域，导致模型在细粒度任务中表现受限。

Method: 提出SubViT，通过在判别性强的图像块中生成多个子标记以增强局部表示，同时保留原始标记序列以维持全局上下文；采用两阶段训练：第一阶段使用来自随机注意力头的分割区域微调模型，引入多样化的分割模式；第二阶段通过特征退化距离识别重要注意力图，并蒸馏为轻量级单图路由器，实现无需额外前向传播的确定性标记重要性预测。

Result: 在CUB、FGVC-Aircraft和Stanford Cars数据集上，SubViT将DINOv2的平均新类别准确率从81.3%提升至84.7%，仅增加0.50毫秒延迟和3.4% FLOPs，且比Retina Patch减少73.8%延迟；在CIFAR-10和ImageNet-100上验证了其广泛适用性。

Conclusion: SubViT通过选择性地增加关键区域的标记容量，在不显著增加计算成本的前提下，显著提升了细粒度视觉识别性能，尤其在需要新类别泛化能力的任务中表现优异，展示了其在高效与高精度之间的良好平衡。

Abstract: We present Subtoken Vision Transformer (SubViT), a selective image tokenization method for fine-grained visual recognition. Standard Vision Transformers compress each fixed-size patch into a single token, although fine-grained distinctions often depend on localized variations within only a few patches. SubViT addresses this mismatch by representing discriminative patches with multiple subtokens while retaining the original token sequence for global context, thereby allocating additional capacity where it is most needed. Since attention heads encode complementary semantics and extracting attention maps at inference requires an extra backbone forward, we adopt a two-stage training strategy. Stage 1 fine-tunes the ViT using subdivision regions sampled from random attention heads, exposing the model to diverse subdivision patterns. Stage 2 identifies informative attention maps through feature-degradation distances and distills them into a lightweight single-map router, which directly predicts deterministic token-importance scores without a separate attention forward. We evaluate SubViT on Generalized Category Discovery (GCD), a challenging task requiring both fine-grained discrimination and generalization to unlabeled novel categories. Across CUB, FGVC-Aircraft, and Stanford Cars, SubViT improves the average novel-category accuracy of DINOv2 from $81.3\%$ to $84.7\%$, with only $0.50$ ms additional latency and $3.4\%$ more FLOPs, while reducing latency by $73.8\%$ relative to Retina Patch. Results on CIFAR-10 and ImageNet-100 demonstrate its broader applicability.

</details>

*Chunggi Lee,Seonwook Park,Wanhua Li,Umar Iqbal,Hanspeter Pfister*

Existing methods rely on pretrained human detection modules, increasing their runtime and limiting the number of tracked entities. We present DETRAM, a unified framework for multi-person HMR and tracking that simultaneously detects, reconstructs, and tracks humans across time, both automatically and via user prompts. DETRAM uses a single transformer decoder with an identity-consistent set of learnable query embeddings that persist across frames: detection queries discover new people, tracking queries maintain pose and shape for existing individuals, and prompt queries follow user-specified identities. Our approach achieves state-of-the-art tracking results on PoseTrack21, 3DPW, BEDLAM, and MuPoTS-3D, and competitive reconstruction accuracy on BEDLAM and 3DPW, while uniquely supporting prompt-based tracking of individuals in multi-person scenes. ### [22] [Beyond Time Shifts: Adapting Omni-LLM as a Reference-Free Evaluator for Generative Audio-Visual Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09091)
*Yijie Qian,Juncheng Wang,Chao Xu,Huihan Wang,Yuxiang Feng,Yang Liu,Baigui Sun,Yong Liu,Shujun Wang*

Motivation: 现有评估指标假设生成内容结构正确，仅关注时间对齐，无法有效评估存在结构幻觉和跨模态关系不对称的生成结果；而人类评估依赖参考对比，自动化指标需无参考绝对评分，二者矛盾导致当前评估严重依赖人工标注，亟需一种能融合人类感知且具备全局一致性的自动评估方法。

Method: 提出SynthSync数据集，通过成对人类标注收集生成失败案例的相对排序；利用配备连续潜在投影的Omni-LLM将相对排名转化为连续绝对分数；设计Real-Valued Group Relative Policy Optimization ($\\mathbb{R}$-GRPO) 方法，通过列表级得分分布内化同步性的全局因果结构，构建可泛化的评估指标。

Result: 所提出的评估指标在与人类偏好对齐方面达到当前最优表现；成功建立标准化基准，使音视频生成评估从低层次信号相关性跃升至视觉基础的因果一致性层面。

Conclusion: 本研究通过融合人类感知与机器学习，构建了一个可解释、可扩展的跨模态同步评估框架，突破了传统指标的局限，为未来世界模拟器的可信生成评估提供了新范式。

Abstract: As audio-visual generative models evolve into world simulators, cross-modal synchronization stands as a critical proxy for assessing the consistency of world dynamics and causality in generated content. However, existing evaluation metrics presume structural correctness, reducing synchronization to mere temporal alignment. Consequently, they fail on generative outputs, especially when exhibiting structural hallucinations and asymmetric cross-modal relations, which currently \textbf{mandate expert human annotation to assess synchronization.} This dependency introduces a critical paradox: \emph{human evaluators rely on relative, reference-dependent comparisons, whereas automated metrics require reference-free, absolute scalars.} We resolve this paradox by proposing a framework that distills relative human perception into a continuous, globally consistent metric. First, we introduce SynthSync, a dataset of generative failures ranked via pairwise human annotations. Second, we adapt the Omni-LLM equipped with a continuous latent projection to translate relative human rankings into continuous absolute values. Third, we propose Real-Valued Group Relative Policy Optimization ($\mathbb{R}$-GRPO) to internalize the global causal structure of synchronization via listwise score distributions. Empirically, our metric achieves state-of-the-art human preference alignment. We leverage this estimator to establish a standardized benchmark, advancing AV-Gen assessment from low-level signal correlation to visually grounded causality.

</details>


### [23] [A Coreset Selection Framework with Ensemble Aggregation for Image Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09100)
*Pedro Rocha Dantas,Lucas Pascotti Valem*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种结合共核选择与多轮集成的框架，用于在大规模图像数据集上高效训练模型。通过分区采样策略（SCOSS）选择代表性子集，并利用多轮独立采样结果进行预测集成，显著提升训练效率与准确性，尤其在标签样本较少时表现优异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模图像数据导致模型训练面临时间和内存开销问题，而现有方法难以准确评估样本贡献且性能不稳定。因此需要一种更稳健、高效的子集选择方法。

Method: 提出SCOSS（SCOre-Stratified Selection）方法，将数据按评分分区间采样，并结合多轮独立训练的集成预测，以增强鲁棒性与代表性。

Result: 实验表明，SCOSS在多种采样比例下表现良好，尤其在SGC分类器中优于基线方法；在细粒度数据集上，使用少量标签样本时，其性能超越SVM。

Abstract: The rapid growth of image data has produced large-scale datasets, raising concerns about the time and memory costs of model training. Selecting representative training subsets, however, remains challenging: individual sample contributions are unclear, and model behavior varies across datasets and runs. We address these challenges with a framework that combines coreset selection with an ensemble aggregation over multiple runs. For coreset selection, we propose SCOre-Stratified Selection (SCOSS), which partitions the training data into intervals based on a chosen score and samples from each interval. The ensemble combines predictions from multiple runs, each performed on an independently sampled training subset. As baselines, we use moderate and random selection, each in original and class-balanced versions. We assess the framework with Simple Graph Convolution (SGC) and Support Vector Machine (SVM) classifiers under different sampling ratios. Experiments show that SCOSS is competitive with baselines, often the best choice for SGC, and enables favorable trade-offs between accuracy and efficiency. On the fine-grained dataset, SGC with SCOSS outperforms SVMs when using fewer labeled samples. The code and supplementary materials are publicly available at http://scoss.lucasvalem.com.

### [24] [Equivariant Filter for High Performance Image Tracking using an Event Camera](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09103)
*Angus Apps,Yixiao Ge,Timothy L. Molloy,Robert Mahony*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于事件相机的等变滤波器设计，用于高精度跟踪平面图像变换。该方法利用AEB追踪器从原始事件流中提取特征位置测量值，并通过具有特殊欧几里得群对称性的等变滤波器计算仿射平移和旋转。滤波器包含一个等效测量更新步骤，有效去除了AEB追踪器提供的高度时间相关特征位置测量值之间的相关性。实验在涉及一般和快速旋转运动的两个数据集上进行评估，结果优于直接优化和协方差交叉方法，在图像平面上特征速度高达7000像素/秒时仍能实现平滑跟踪。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统图像跟踪方法在高速运动下易受事件数据高度时间相关性的影响，导致跟踪性能下降。为提升高速场景下的跟踪精度与稳定性，需设计一种能有效处理事件流相关性的高效滤波框架。

Method: 结合Asynchronous Event Blob (AEB)追踪器提取特征位置，采用基于特殊欧几里得群对称性的等变滤波器，引入等效测量更新步骤以消除事件数据的时间相关性，从而实现对图像平移与旋转的精确估计。

Result: 所提方法在两个数据集上均表现出优异性能，可稳定跟踪图像平面上速度高达7000像素/秒的特征，显著优于直接优化和协方差交叉方法，且轨迹更加平滑。

Conclusion: 本研究提出的等变滤波器设计有效克服了事件相机输出的高度时间相关性问题，实现了高速、高精度的图像跟踪，适用于自动驾驶与机器人等实时视觉应用。

Abstract: Image tracking is the problem of estimating the transformation that relates a moving image of a scene to an original reference image. The problem is important in control of autonomous vehicles or robots, where the image encodes information about the motion of the camera or environment, as well as in pure computer vision applications. In this paper, we present an equivariant filter design for high performance tracking of planar image transformations using an event camera. The design exploits the Asynchronous Event Blob (AEB) tracker (Wang et al., 2024) to extract feature-position measurements from the raw event stream, and an equivariant filter to compute an affine image translation and rotation using the special Euclidean group symmetry. The equivariant filter incorporates an equivalent-measurement update step that de-correlates the (highly temporally correlated) feature-position measurements provided by the AEB tracker. We evaluate the design experimentally using two datasets involving general and fast rotational motion. We benchmark results against direct optimisation (estimating the relative transformation from the raw blob tracks), and a covariance intersection approach for overcoming data correlation. Our design provides smooth image tracking for features moving up to 7000 pixels per second on the image plane.

Method: 使用视觉语言模型（VLM）生成图像的文本描述，再由大型语言模型（LLM）评估图像间的语义相似度，基于此相似度对kNN和互近邻图进行边裁剪，去除语义无关连接，从而构建更高质量的图结构，并将其用于后续的半监督图像分类任务。

Result: 实验结果显示，利用LLM进行图结构优化可有效提升分类准确率，尤其是在kNN图和部分骨干网络上效果显著。该方法在保持原有框架基础上提升了模型性能，且具有良好的泛化潜力。

Conclusion: 将大型语言模型与图卷积网络结合，通过语义驱动的方式优化图像图结构，是提升半监督图像分类性能的有效途径。本方法为跨模态信息融合在视觉任务中的应用提供了新思路，未来可拓展至更多下游任务。

Abstract: While the growing availability of image data has driven significant advances, labeling datasets remains costly and time-consuming. Therefore, semi-supervised approaches such as Graph Convolutional Networks (GCNs), which learn from both labeled and unlabeled data, have emerged as a promising solution. One of the primary challenges in applying GCNs to image classification is graph construction, since, unlike in citation networks or similar domains, images typically do not come with a predefined structural representation. For visual data, most studies construct graphs based on the similarity between feature vectors from pretrained deep learning backbones, typically by employing kNN or reciprocal kNN algorithms. Although Large Language Models (LLMs) have shown remarkable capability in capturing high-level semantics, their integration with GCNs for image classification remains underexplored. Aiming to fill this gap, our approach uses a Vision Language Model (VLM) to generate textual image descriptions, which are then processed by an LLM to estimate semantic similarity scores between connected images. These scores guide the pruning of edges in kNN and reciprocal kNN graphs, filtering out semantically irrelevant neighbors. Experimental results reveal that leveraging LLMs for graph refinement can improve classification accuracy, particularly for kNN graphs and some backbones. The source code is publicly available at http://gcnllm.lucasvalem.com.

Abstract: Video anomaly detection (VAD) is critical for automated surveillance but remains fragile under challenging conditions such as illumination variations, fast motion, and complex backgrounds when relying solely on visible light videos. To address these limitations, we propose EVAD, an event enhanced VAD framework that jointly exploits conventional video and event streams captured by bio inspired event cameras. Event sensors asynchronously capture brightness changes with high temporal resolution, offering robustness to motion blur and extreme lighting, and providing motion salient cues complementary to video based visual information. To support multi modal VAD research, we construct a large scale visible event benchmark comprising 6.3 billion events and 376,368 video frames collected under diverse illumination levels, motion patterns, and background complexities, filling the gap of realistic and scalable datasets for event based anomaly detection. An adaptive fusion module then dynamically integrates event based temporal cues with video based spatial semantics, improving robustness to environmental disturbances. Experiments on Phoenix-2014T, CSL-Daily, How2Sign, and OpenASL demonstrate consistent state-of-the-art performance, with ablations confirming the complementary contributions of each component. ### [28] [Event Burst Trigger: An Availability Backdoor Attack on Event-Based SNN Object Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09115)
*Jaesun Baek,Chanwook Lee,Eun-Kyu Lee*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种针对基于脉冲神经网络（SNN）的事件视觉目标检测模型的可用性后门攻击方法——事件爆发触发（EBT）。该攻击通过在训练数据中注入精心设计的事件触发，使推理时产生时间集中型事件流，导致大量虚假目标候选，从而显著增加后处理阶段（尤其是非极大值抑制，NMS）的计算开销。实验表明，尽管检测精度几乎不受影响（mAP@0.5下降小于0.099），但NMS延迟最高上升38%，凸显了其在事件驱动SNN系统中的可用性瓶颈。此外，在边缘平台上，该攻击提升了资源利用率并减少了调度余量，且不易被现有检测方法识别，揭示了事件视觉SNN系统中一个未被充分关注的可用性威胁。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前事件视觉与脉冲神经网络（SNN）在边缘智能中广泛应用，但其在严格时延与能效约束下的安全性研究不足，尤其对可用性后门攻击缺乏深入探讨。现有研究多关注功能完整性，而忽视系统响应能力的破坏。因此，亟需评估此类攻击对实时性敏感的事件驱动系统的影响。

Method: 提出事件爆发触发（EBT）攻击：在训练数据中嵌入特定事件模式作为触发器，诱导推理阶段出现突发性事件流；利用该流生成大量伪目标候选，进而放大非极大值抑制（NMS）的计算负担；攻击无需修改模型结构、损失函数或推理流程，符合毒化仅（poison-only）威胁模型。

Result: 实验结果显示，检测精度保持稳定（mAP@0.5下降<0.099），但NMS阶段延迟最高提升38%；在边缘平台验证中，资源使用率上升，调度余量减少，无明显资源峰值；现有的STRIP检测方法无法有效区分攻击样本与正常输入。

Conclusion: EBT揭示了事件驱动SNN目标检测系统中一种新型可用性后门威胁，即通过隐蔽触发引发计算负载激增，损害系统实时性能，而对准确率影响极小。这表明在设计安全可靠的边缘智能系统时，必须考虑此类隐蔽性高、影响大的可用性攻击风险。

Abstract: Event-based vision and spiking neural networks (SNNs) are increasingly adopted for edge intelligence under strict latency and energy constraints. However, the vulnerability of event-based SNN object detection models to availability backdoor attacks remains insufficiently studied. This paper presents Event Burst Trigger (EBT), an availability backdoor attack targeting SNN-based object detection models. EBT injects carefully crafted event-based triggers into the training data, which induce temporally concentrated event streams during inference. These burst-like activations increase the number of phantom (i.e., spurious) object candidates, and consequently inflate the computational cost of the post-processing stage, particularly Non-Maximum Suppression (NMS). We evaluate EBT on SpikeYOLO, the state-of-the-art SNN-based object detector, under a poison-only threat model that does not require modifications to the model architecture, loss function, or inference pipeline. Experimental results show that while detection accuracy remains largely preserved, with mAP@0.5 decreasing by less than 0.099, the latency of the NMS stage increases by up to 38%. This indicates that NMS can become a dominant availability bottleneck in event-based SNN object detection. Experiments on an edge platform further show that the proposed attack elevates baseline resource utilization and reduces scheduling slack without inducing conspicuous peaks in resource usage. In addition, STRIP-based backdoor detection fails to reliably distinguish the proposed attack from benign inputs. These results characterize a previously underexplored availability backdoor threat in event-based SNN object detection systems.

### [29] [4D Human-Scene Reconstruction from Low-Overlap Captures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09125)
*Minhyuk Hwang,Sangmin Kim,Seunguk Do,Daneul Kim,Jaesik Park*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出StudioRecon，一种从稀疏、低重叠摄像头重建4D人类场景的管道，通过解耦背景与人类实现。利用视频扩散模型合成数百个受控新视角以增强背景监督，通过跨视图身份关联和多视角关键点拟合稳健初始化可变形高斯人体，再通过运动自适应一致性注入的递归增强模块优化输出，有效减少未观测区域的伪影。在四个真实数据集上达到最先进的新视角合成效果，并支持新轨迹渲染和人体替换等应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有动态人体体积捕捉依赖密集相机阵列以实现高保真度，但在实际场景中仅能获得少量低重叠摄像头，导致输出质量下降且存在大片未观测区域。尽管近期4D重建方法关注低重叠设置，仍存在显著伪影；视频扩散模型虽为替代方案，但对人类几何表现不一致。因此需要一种能在稀疏低重叠条件下实现高质量4D重建的方法。

Method: 提出StudioRecon管道：1）通过视频扩散模型生成大量受控新视角以增强背景监督；2）利用跨视图身份关联和三角化多视角关键点拟合初始化可变形高斯人体；3）采用递归增强模块结合运动自适应一致性注入，优化整体输出，减少残余伪影。

Result: 在四个真实世界数据集上实现了最先进的新视角合成性能；成功应用于新轨迹渲染和人体替换任务，显著提升稀疏低重叠条件下的4D重建质量与几何一致性。

Conclusion: StudioRecon通过背景-人体解耦、增强背景监督、稳健人体初始化及递归一致性优化，在稀疏低重叠摄像头条件下实现了高质量4D人体重建，为真实场景中的动态人体捕捉提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Existing volumetric capture of dynamic human performance achieves high fidelity with dense camera arrays. However, in real-world scenarios, only a handful of low-overlap cameras are available, which degrades the output quality and leaves large areas unobserved. Recent 4D reconstruction methods have focused on low-overlap settings, yet they still produce noticeable artifacts in under-observed regions. Video diffusion models have emerged as another option, but they show geometrically inconsistent results for humans. To address these limitations, we propose StudioRecon, a pipeline that reconstructs 4D human scenes from sparse, low-overlap cameras by decoupling background and humans. We densify background supervision by synthesizing hundreds of camera-controlled novel views with a video diffusion model. We also robustly initialize deformable Gaussian humans with cross-view identity association and triangulated multi-view keypoint fitting. Finally, our recursive enhancement module with motion-adaptive consistency injection harmonizes the composed output, thereby further avoiding remaining artifacts. We achieve state-of-the-art novel view synthesis across four real-world datasets and demonstrate applications such as novel trajectory rendering and human replacement.

</details>

However, existing frameworks remain subjugated by a coarse-grained blind injection paradigm that perpetually enforces a globally static guidance strength while indiscriminately sampling the supervisor timestep. This state-agnostic design completely disregards the intrinsic nature of image generation as a dynamic evolutionary process characterized by progressive entropy reduction, which not only restricts the performance boundary of few-step compression but also precipitates severe CFG over-conditioning artifacts. To transcend these limitations, we re-examine the distillation procedure through the theoretical lens of Information Theory, formally modeling it as a dynamic mutual information game constrained by the Information Bottleneck (IB) principle. To regulate the injection strength, we introduce an entropy-aware schedule that dynamically decays alongside the SNR, applying maximal thrust for initial structural anchoring before smoothly reverting to the natural manifold to refine micro-details. Extensive empirical evaluations corroborate that our framework fundamentally eradicates over-conditioning artifacts, shattering the performance ceiling to achieve SOTA generative fidelity under extremely stringent 2-step configurations.

### [32] [Weaving Light and Time: Unified Harmonic-Geometric Representation Learning for Dense RGB-Event Parsing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09143)
*Chenxu Peng,Chongtian zhou,Dicheng Liu,Bo-Wen Yin,Yimian Dai,Xialei Liu,Ming-Ming Cheng,Xiang Li*

Method: 提出 Evita 统一主干网络，包含三个核心模块：几何畸变校正（Geometric Parallax Rectification）实现自适应空间对齐；谐波频域共振（Harmonic Spectral Resonance）在复数频率域完成纹理迁移；瞬态全局路由（Transient Global Routing）实现事件驱动的非对称注意力机制。同时构建 N-ImageNetV2 数据集并设计随机事件表示混合预训练协议，增强模型对多种事件格式的泛化能力。

Conclusion: Evita 成功实现了针对 RGB-Event 多模态感知的高效统一建模，解决了传统方法在模态融合中的关键瓶颈，为复杂环境下的实时感知提供了新范式。代码已开源，便于后续研究与应用。

Abstract: Fusing standard RGB frames with asynchronous event streams has emerged as a definitive paradigm for robust perception in degraded environments. Although unified backbones have recently gained traction in multi-modal vision, adapting them to the RGB-Event domain remains fundamentally challenging. Existing architectures either resort to decoupled dual encoders that double computational overhead, or adopt generic unified designs that fail to resolve implicit geometric parallax and cross-spectral aliasing under the extreme representational divide between dense intensity grids and sparse kinematic spikes. To transcend these bottlenecks, we present Evita, the first unified backbone specifically engineered for dedicated dense RGB-Event parsing. To achieve profound modal synergy, Evita explicitly embeds a suite of intrinsic co-learning modules directly into every encoder layer. Specifically, it features Geometric Parallax Rectification for adaptive spatial alignment, Harmonic Spectral Resonance for texture transfer exclusively in the complex frequency domain, and Transient Global Routing for event-driven asymmetric attention. To guarantee robust feature extraction against spatial misalignments and decouple representations from specific event encodings, we construct N-ImageNetV2 alongside a stochastic event representation mixing pretraining protocol, empowering the network to seamlessly accommodate arbitrary event formats in downstream tasks. Extensive evaluations across the DELIVER, DDD17, and DSEC benchmarks confirm that Evita establishes new state-of-the-art metrics while delivering a superior accuracy-latency trade-off for real-time multimodal perception.The code are publicly available at: https://github.com/chaineypung/Evita.

### [33] [What Pixels Are Enough? SEAMS: Sufficiency Saliency via MSE-Preservation Soft-Masks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09164)
*Magdalena Trędowicz,Łukasz Struski,Arkadiusz Lewicki,Karolina Pachota,Andrzej Grudzień,Mateusz Jagła,Jacek Tabor*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: SEAMS是一种基于充分性的显著性方法，通过优化软掩码来直接保留模型输出，无需额外数据集或特定架构的归因机制。它使用可学习的预算和仅来自查询图像的三路图像合成，能够生成对象级、类别条件和标记级解释，且结果紧凑、可解释、稳定，并在插入/删除基准测试中表现良好。不同架构依赖不同的充分证据，表明视觉解释具有架构依赖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有显著性方法通常关注必要性而非充分性，即关注哪些区域对模型预测不可或缺，但忽视了哪些区域足以维持模型行为。为提升解释的实用性，需要一种能识别足够信息区域的方法，从而提供更简洁、更具可解释性的解释。

Method: SEAMS采用基于软掩码的优化框架，利用可学习的预算和完全由查询图像生成的三路复合图像，直接优化一个软掩码以保持指定模型输出（如类别概率、嵌入或标记表示）。该方法不依赖辅助数据集、特定架构的归因机制或可微分的top-k近似。

Result: SEAMS在ViT-S/16和ConvNeXt模型上均表现出色，能通过调整目标输出生成多种粒度的解释（对象级、类别条件、标记级），生成的掩码紧凑、可解释、对随机初始化稳定，且在插入/删除基准测试中表现与现有方法相当甚至更优。实验还发现不同架构依赖不同的充分证据，说明视觉解释具有架构依赖性。

Conclusion: SEAMS提供了一种通用、高效且可解释的显著性方法，能够基于充分性原则生成高质量解释，同时揭示了不同深度模型在解释上的本质差异，强调了架构设计对解释性的影响。

Abstract: Saliency maps are most useful when they identify the image regions that are sufficient to preserve a model's behaviour. We introduce SEAMS, a sufficiency-based saliency method that directly optimises a soft mask using a preservation objective. Given a frozen differentiable model output, such as a class probability, CLS embedding, or token representation, SEAMS searches for a compact mask that preserves the selected output. The approach relies on a simple optimisation framework based on soft masks, a learnable budget, and a three-way image composite generated entirely from the query image. As a result, it requires no auxiliary distractor dataset, architecture-specific attribution mechanism, or differentiable top-k relaxation. Experiments with frozen ViT-S/16 and ConvNeXt models show that the same optimisation pipeline can generate object-level, class-conditioned, and token-level explanations by changing only the preserved target. The resulting masks are compact, interpretable, stable across random initialisations, and competitive on insertion and deletion benchmarks. Our results also indicate that different architectures often rely on different sufficient evidence while achieving similar preservation fidelity, highlighting the architecture-dependent nature of visual explanations.

### [34] [TSR-Ego: Temporally Guided Stereo Refinement Framework for Egocentric 3D Human Pose Estimation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09169)
*Md Mushfiqur Azam,John Quarles,Kevin Desai*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: TSR-Ego提出一种时序引导的立体框架，通过结合短期运动证据与投影引导的特征采样，提升头戴式立体相机下的3D人体姿态估计性能。该方法利用因果深度可分离卷积增强时序特征，并在单阶段解码器中通过时序自注意力、关节自注意力和鱼眼可变形立体交叉注意力，动态生成2D采样参考点，从而在弱立体线索或遮挡情况下仍保持鲁棒性。实验表明，在UnrealEgo2和UnrealEgo-RW数据集上达到当前最优表现，尤其在真实世界序列中优势显著。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有立体头戴式人体姿态估计方法依赖帧内局部证据，仅将时间信息作为辅助上下文，导致在当前帧立体线索弱、遮挡或模糊时性能下降。需要更有效融合时序运动信息以提升鲁棒性。

Method: 提出TSR-Ego框架，首先使用因果深度可分离卷积对密集立体特征图进行时序增强，引入历史视觉证据；随后采用单阶段因果立体解码器，通过时序自注意力、关节自注意力及鱼眼可变形立体交叉注意力，利用演化姿态估计生成2D采样参考，实现特征与关节表示的联合优化。

Result: 在UnrealEgo2和UnrealEgo-RW数据集上取得当前最优性能，尤其在真实世界序列中表现突出，验证了时序引导策略的有效性与鲁棒性。

Abstract: Egocentric 3D human pose estimation from head-mounted stereo cameras is challenging due to fisheye distortion, severe self-occlusion, and frequent truncation of body joints outside the camera field of view. Recent stereo egocentric methods have improved performance through heatmap lifting, stereo correspondence, and transformer-based refinement, but they often rely heavily on frame-local evidence or use temporal information only as auxiliary pose-level context. This limits robustness when current-frame stereo cues are weak, occluded, or ambiguous. We propose TSR-Ego, a temporally guided stereo framework that couples short-term motion evidence with projection-guided feature sampling. The model first enriches dense stereo feature maps using a causal depthwise-separable temporal convolution, allowing past visual evidence to influence the feature space before deformable cross-attention. A single-stage causal stereo decoder then refines learned 3D joint queries through temporal self-attention, joint self-attention, and fisheye deformable stereo cross-attention, using the evolving pose estimate to generate 2D sampling references. Unlike methods that apply temporal reasoning mainly after pose prediction, TSR-Ego uses motion context to shape both the sampled stereo features and the joint representations while preserving online inference without future frames. Experiments on UnrealEgo2 and UnrealEgo-RW show state-of-the-art performance, with especially strong gains on real-world sequences.

### [35] [Causally Debiased Latent Action Model for Embodied Action Conditioned World Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09185)
*Yufan Wei,Kun Zhou,Lingjun Mao,Zijun Zhang,Ziming Xu,Ziqiao Xi,Shuang Liang,Ruobing Han,Yuchen Yan,Xinyue Wang,Fan Feng,Biwei Huang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出CD-LAM框架，包含三个核心微调目标：(1) 以实体为中心的重建，强调对机器人自身及其交互对象的关注；(2) 以动作为中心的对比学习，增强潜在动作表示对动作变化的敏感性；(3) 潜在空间校准，防止潜在表示坍缩，确保其结构化与可解释性。通过联合优化这三个目标，使潜在动作表征更专注、更准确、更具鲁棒性。

Result: 在2B和14B规模的ACWM骨干网络上，CD-LAM显著提升了潜在动作可控性、下游机器人动作跟随性能、视觉重建质量以及适应效率；仅需6000次微调步骤，且相比基线减少超过12倍的机器人动作适应更新次数，验证了其高效性和实用性。

Conclusion: CD-LAM成功解决了潜在动作模型中的动作无关偏差问题，实现了更可控、更精准、更高效的行动条件世界建模，为机器人规划与策略评估提供了坚实基础，具有显著的工程应用潜力。

Abstract: Action-conditioned world models (ACWMs) aim to simulate future observations conditioned on embodied actions, offering a promising foundation for robot planning, policy evaluation, and data augmentation. However, learning controllable ACWMs requires large-scale action-labeled data, which remains costly to collect in the real world. Latent action models (LAMs) mitigate this bottleneck by inferring latent actions from unlabeled videos, but existing LAMs are typically trained with reconstruction-only objectives and therefore entangle action-relevant dynamics with action-irrelevant visual factors such as backgrounds and untouched objects. In this work, we identify this action-irrelevant bias as a key obstacle to controllable ACWMs and introduce evaluation metrics to measure latent-action bias, action following, and robustness. We propose CD-LAM, a causally debiased framework for LAM-based ACWMs. CD-LAM introduces three efficient fine-tuning objectives: embodiment-centric reconstruction, action-centric contrastive learning, and latent space calibration, which together encourage embodiment-focused, action-aware, and calibrated non-collapsed latent action representations. Experiments on 2B and 14B ACWM backbones show that CD-LAM substantially improves latent-action controllability, downstream robot-action following, visual fidelity, and adaptation efficiency, requiring only 6k fine-tuning steps and more than 12$\times$ fewer robot-action adaptation updates than the baseline.

### [36] [HiHR: Hierarchical Hyperbolic Representation for Aerial-Ground Person Re-Identification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09186)
*Qiwei Yang,Pingping Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出了一种用于空中-地面行人重识别（AG-ReID）的分层双曲表示（HiHR）框架，通过多粒度特征融合与双曲空间中的层次化特征结构，有效整合视图不变和视图特定判别特征，在四个基准上验证了其优越性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法直接对齐跨视角特征，忽略了视图特有线索，导致性能受限。

Method: 采用预训练视觉-文本编码器提取多粒度特征，设计文本引导的多粒度融合（TMF）增强身份特征表达，并引入分层双曲学习（HHL）在双曲空间构建包含粗粒度（保证身份可分性与跨视角一致性）和细粒度（保留视图特定判别线索）的层次结构。

Abstract: Aerial-Ground Person Re-IDentification (AG-ReID) aims to retrieve the same person across heterogeneous aerial and ground camera platforms. Although great progress has been made, existing methods remain suboptimal due to the direct feature alignment across views, overlooking view-specific cues. To address this issue, we propose a novel Hierarchical Hyperbolic Representation (HiHR) framework for AG-ReID. More specifically, we first extract multi-granularity features based on pre-trained visual-text encoders. Then, we propose a Text-guided Multi-granularity Fusion (TMF) to fuse multi-granularity features and enhance the representation ability of identity features. Furthermore, we introduce the Hierarchical Hyperbolic Learning (HHL) to construct a hierarchical feature structure in a hyperbolic space. This hierarchy includes a coarse level that ensures identity separability and cross-view consistency, and a fine level that preserves view-specific discriminative cues. As a result, our proposed framework can effectively aggregate view-invariant and view-specific discriminative features for AG-ReID. Extensive experiments on four AG-ReID benchmarks demonstrate the effectiveness of our framework. The source code is available at https://github.com/YangQiWei3/HiHR.

</details>


### [37] [YeTI: You Only Need Two Noisy Images for Real-World sRGB Noise Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09193)
*Jaekyun Ko,Byung Wan Lim,Soomin Lee,Dongjin Kim,Tae Hyun Kim*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: YeTI是一种无需干净图像或相机元数据的实时sRGB噪声生成框架，仅需两幅同一场景的噪声图像即可学习真实世界噪声特性。它通过重建自编码器分离场景结构与噪声，并使用基于一致性目标的一步条件扩散变换器建模噪声分布。在推理时，给定单张噪声输入，可生成信号依赖的真实噪声，同时保留场景内容。在SIDD、SIDD+、MAI2021和SID等基准上验证了其有效性，且在DND上的去噪任务中表现优异，证明了该方法在无监督噪声生成中的实用价值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 真实世界sRGB图像去噪因传感器噪声的非线性特性以及难以获取对齐的干净-噪声图像对而具有挑战性。监督方法容易在有限配对数据集上过拟合，自监督方法则仍依赖于足够多样的噪声观测。因此需要一种无需干净图像或相机元数据的可扩展噪声合成方法来建模真实噪声。

Method: YeTI利用重建自编码器分离场景结构与噪声特征，并采用一步条件扩散变换器结合一致性目标建模潜在噪声分布。仅需两幅同一场景的噪声图像进行训练，推理时可基于单张噪声输入生成真实的信号依赖噪声。

Result: YeTI在SIDD、SIDD+、MAI2021和SID等多个真实世界图像去噪基准上表现出色，下游去噪模型在DND数据集上也取得了强性能，表明其在无干净图像、无元数据条件下生成高质量噪声的有效性与实用性。

Conclusion: YeTI成功实现了无需干净图像和相机元数据的真实世界噪声生成，为真实图像去噪提供了有效的数据增强手段，具备良好的泛化能力和实际应用价值。

Abstract: Real-world sRGB image denoising remains challenging due to the nonlinear characteristics of sensor noise and the difficulty of acquiring aligned clean-noisy image pairs. Supervised denoisers often overfit to limited paired datasets, while self-supervised methods still depend on sufficiently diverse noisy observations. These limitations motivate scalable noise synthesis methods that can model real-world noise without clean ground truth or camera metadata. We propose YeTI, a real-world sRGB noise generation framework that learns from only two noisy observations of the same scene. YeTI uses a Reconstruction Autoencoder to disentangle scene structure and noise characteristics, and models the latent noise distribution with a one-step Conditional Diffusion Transformer trained using consistency objectives. Given a single noisy input at inference time, YeTI generates realistic, signal-dependent noise while preserving the underlying scene content. Extensive experiments demonstrate the effectiveness of YeTI across real-world benchmarks. We evaluate noise generation on SIDD and further assess generalization on SIDD+, MAI2021, and SID, covering smartphone and diverse consumer-camera sensors. Downstream denoising results on DND further show that denoisers trained with YeTI-synthesized images achieve strong real-world performance, highlighting the practical value of clean-image-free and metadata-free noise generation.

### [38] [Glob3R: Global Structure-from-Motion with 3D Foundation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09225)
*Junyuan Deng,Heng Li,Kejie Qiu,Lingteng Qiu,Rui Peng,Weichao Shen,Weihao Yuan,Siyu Zhu,Zilong Dong,Ping Tan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Glob3R是一种基于3D基础模型的全局SfM式重建方法，通过显式优化前馈几何预测，利用轻量级密集匹配头生成图像形变，转换为稀疏但可靠的多视图特征轨迹，并结合关键帧滑动窗口策略实现可扩展重建。通过全局运动平均和束调整进一步优化相机位姿，减少尺度不一致，恢复稠密场景几何。在多个基准测试中表现优异，优于现有前馈模型和可扩展重建方法，且比传统SfM更鲁棒，同时提升神经渲染质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有3D基础模型如VGGT虽能实现高效的前馈3D重建，但存在精度不足的问题，且在处理长序列或无序图像集时通常需分块处理，易引入漂移与不一致性。因此，亟需一种能够结合基础模型先验与全局几何优化的可扩展、高精度重建方法。

Method: Glob3R采用冻结的Pi3X骨干网络，增加轻量级密集匹配头以预测参考帧与邻近视图间的图像形变；将这些密集形变转化为稀疏但可靠的多视图特征轨迹，提供对应约束用于全局优化；引入基于关键帧的滑动窗口关联策略，实现轨迹与相对位姿在重叠窗口间的传播；最后进行全局运动平均与束调整，以优化相机位姿、消除尺度偏差并恢复稠密几何结构。

Result: Glob3R在室内、室外、大规模驾驶及无序SfM基准上均实现了鲁棒且准确的重建性能，显著优于前馈基础模型基线与近期可扩展重建方法，且比经典SfM更具鲁棒性；优化后的位姿也显著提升了神经渲染质量，验证了融合基础模型先验与全局几何优化的有效性。

Conclusion: Glob3R成功将3D基础模型的高效前馈能力与全局几何优化相结合，实现了高精度、可扩展、鲁棒的3D重建，为大规模场景重建提供了新范式，尤其适用于复杂真实场景下的神经渲染与重建任务。

Abstract: Recent 3D geometric foundation models, such as VGGT, provide robust feed-forward 3D reconstruction by directly predicting camera poses and 3D scene points from input images. However, their results remain inaccurate, and scaling them to long sequences or large unordered image sets typically requires chunk-wise processing, which can introduce drift and inconsistency. We present Glob3R, a global SfM-style reconstruction built on 3D foundation models. Our key idea is to explicitly optimize feed-forward geometric predictions. To this end, we augment a frozen Pi3X backbone with a lightweight dense matching head that predicts image warps between selected reference frames and neighboring views. These dense warps are converted into sparse but reliable multi-view feature tracks, which provide correspondence constraints for global optimization. We further introduce a keyframe-based sliding-window association strategy that propagates tracks and relative poses across overlapping windows, enabling scalable reconstruction. Finally, we perform global motion averaging and bundle adjustment to refine camera poses, reduce scale inconsistencies, and recover dense scene geometry. Extensive experiments on indoor, outdoor, large-scale driving, and unordered SfM benchmarks demonstrate that Glob3R achieves robust and accurate reconstruction. It consistently improves over feed-forward foundation-model baselines and recent scalable reconstruction methods, while being more robust than classical SfM pipelines. The refined poses also lead to higher-quality neural rendering, validating the benefit of combining foundation-model priors with global geometric optimization. Project page: https://junyuandeng.github.io/Glob3r

### [40] [Semantic Hardness Is Not Visual Hardness: Sign-Aware Hard Negative Mining for Sign Language Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09263)
*Junmyeong Lee,Chan Hur,ChangSu Choi,Sukmin Cho,Fitsum Gaim,Eui Jun Hwang,Hoyun Song,KyungTae Lim*

TL;DR: 该研究提出Sign-Aware Hard Negative Mining (SAN)方法，通过在签语言嵌入空间中基于视觉混淆性构建难负样本，解决细粒度手语检索中因现有文本挖掘策略无法捕捉视觉相似性而导致的性能瓶颈。实验表明，SAN显著提升了细粒度检索性能，同时保持了粗粒度准确率，强调了负样本监督与视觉模糊性对齐的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有手语检索方法在细粒度场景下表现脆弱，主要原因并非模型容量不足，而是负样本监督无效；特别是语义不同但视觉相似的手势常未被当作难负样本处理，而传统基于文本的挖掘策略难以捕捉这种视觉模糊性。

Method: 提出Sign-Aware Hard Negative Mining (SAN)，不再依赖语言相似性，而是基于签语言嵌入空间中的视觉混淆性来构建难负样本，以更准确地反映真实视觉混淆情况。

Result: 在PHOENIX-2014T数据集上的实验显示，SAN显著提升了细粒度检索性能，同时维持了原有的粗粒度准确性，验证了视觉模糊性对齐在负样本设计中的关键作用。

Conclusion: 手语检索中的细粒度失败主要源于负样本分布不匹配，通过引入基于视觉混淆性的硬负样本挖掘机制，可有效提升检索性能，表明负样本设计应与视觉实际混淆情况对齐。

Abstract: Sign Language Retrieval (SLRet) enables efficient access to sign language content but remains fragile in fine-grained scenarios where visually similar signs must be distinguished. We show that this limitation does not stem from model capacity, but from ineffective hard negative supervision. Specifically, we formulate fine-grained retrieval failures as a negative distribution mismatch: semantically distinct yet visually confusable signs are rarely treated as hard negatives, while existing text-based mining strategies fail to capture such visual ambiguity. To address this issue, we propose Sign-Aware Hard Negative Mining (SAN), which constructs hard negatives based on visual confusability in the sign embedding space rather than linguistic similarity. Experiments on PHOENIX-2014T demonstrate that SAN substantially improves fine-grained retrieval performance while preserving coarse-grained accuracy, highlighting the importance of aligning negative supervision with visual ambiguity in sign language retrieval.

### [41] [REMIND: RE-Identification with Memory for INDoor Navigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09267)
*Pablo Diaz-Pereda,Alejandro Rodriguez-Ramos,David Perez-Saura,Pascual Campoy*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: REMIND 是一种用于单目RGB图像中长期多对象重识别的在线跟踪器，不依赖相机位姿或深度信息。它结合了冻结的DINOv3特征、双银行多原型外观记忆、部件与背景级描述符、邻居上下文推理模块以及带有模糊性感知保护的联合匈牙利分配机制，有效应对长时间间隔、视角变化和光照变化等挑战。在自建室内数据集上，REMIND 的 IDF1 达到 90.35%，远超现有基线；在 ScanNet++ 上也表现优异，几乎在所有设置中领先，且系统稳定、无内存溢出问题。

  <summary>Details</summary>
