### [123] [Signed Symmetric Quantization for Few-Bit Integers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08779)
*Ian Colbert,Eashan Dash,Pablo Monteagudo-Lago,Juan Amboage,Srinidhi N,Giuseppe Franco,Nicholas J. Fraser,Arun Ramachandran*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的有符号对称量化方法（signed absmax grid），在低比特精度下有效利用了有符号整数表示中额外的负数表示能力，通过轻量级的符号选择规则将多余的表示值分配给主导的异常值尾部，保持零点为零，从而避免了非对称量化带来的运行时开销。理论分析表明该方法在88-99%的模型权重组上满足$\ell_2$误差条件最优性；同时证明了将标准对称量化器的尺度取负等价于在相同有符号整数字母表上进行单位零点偏移。实验验证显示，在Qwen3、Qwen3.5和Llama3系列模型上，该方法在不增加推理成本的前提下，显著提升了困惑度和少样本准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准对称量化因强制正尺度导致有符号整数中额外的负数表示被用于负尾部，可能引发正异常值截断，造成不可忽视的量化误差。尽管非对称量化可通过零点调整缓解此问题，但带来显著运行时开销。因此需要一种既能保留对称量化高效性又可优化表示分配的新方案。

Method: 提出有符号absmax量化网格，基于数据分布动态选择符号方向，使多余负数表示指向主导异常值尾部，同时保持零点为零；通过理论推导证明其在特定条件下$\ell_2$误差最优，并揭示尺度取负与零点偏移的数学等价性。

Result: 在多个主流LLM模型上，所提方法在4位及以下精度下实现了比标准无符号对称量化更低的困惑度和更高的少样本准确率，且无需额外推理开销，性能优于对称与非对称量化。

Conclusion: 有符号对称量化（signed absmax）提供了一种兼具高效率与高精度的低比特量化新范式，尤其适用于资源受限场景下的大语言模型部署。

Abstract: The signed integer alphabet contains one more negative representable value than positive. Yet, by convention, the standard symmetric integer quantizer fixes its scale to be strictly positive, which assigns this extra representable value to the negative tail and can force clipping of positive outliers. In this work, we show that, at few-bit precision, such clipping is a non-trivial source of quantization error. Asymmetric quantization addresses this problem with a zero point, shifting the grid toward the observed data range; however, this flexibility is well-known to carry a runtime penalty. For example, in llama.cpp on an AMD EPYC(TM) "Turin" CPU, a 4-bit symmetric format uses up to 9% less memory with up to 2.45$\times$ higher throughput than its asymmetric counterpart. We highlight signed symmetric quantization as a third option that retains the runtime profile of symmetric quantization without the penalty of the asymmetric format: our signed absmax grid places the extra representable value on the dominant-outlier tail through a principled and lightweight sign selection rule while keeping the zero point at zero. Our theoretical analysis offers two main results. First, we establish the signed absmax grid as conditionally bound-optimal on $\ell_2$ quantization error, and show that the condition holds for 88-99% of weight groups across pre-trained large language models (LLMs) at low bit widths. Second, we show that negating the scale of a standard symmetric quantizer is analytically equivalent to a unit zero point shift on the same signed integer alphabet. We empirically validate our proposal on models from the Qwen3, Qwen3.5, and Llama3 families, and observe improvement in perplexity and downstream few-shot accuracy over the standard unsigned symmetric quantizer at no extra inference cost

</details>


### [124] [Sticky Routing: Training MoE Models for Memory-Efficient Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08780)
*Ali Kayyam*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: StickyMoE introduces a differentiable routing consistency loss to reduce expert switches between adjacent tokens in MoE models, improving efficiency on edge devices without architectural changes. It enables co-adaptation of experts and router from the start of training, reducing switch rates by up to 60% with minimal performance loss.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Consecutive tokens in MoE models often activate different experts, leading to frequent weight swapping between slow storage and fast memory on edge devices, which degrades efficiency. Existing solutions are either system-level or post-hoc, failing to address the root cause during pretraining.

Method: StickyMoE applies a differentiable routing consistency loss that penalizes abrupt expert switches between adjacent tokens, encouraging consistent expert assignment across semantically coherent spans. It requires no architectural changes and introduces only one hyperparameter (lambda).

Result: Experiments show StickyMoE reduces expert switch rate by up to 60% with less than 4% perplexity degradation, outperforming post-hoc fine-tuning in terms of quality-locality trade-off.

Conclusion: Routing temporal locality is most effectively established during training, and StickyMoE achieves this efficiently through a simple, end-to-end trainable loss, offering significant gains in model efficiency without sacrificing performance.

Abstract: Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) models activate only a sparse subset of experts per token, yet consecutive tokens frequently activate different experts -- causing constant weight swapping between slow storage and fast memory on edge devices. Existing remedies are either system-level (caching heuristics) or post-hoc (router fine-tuning), leaving the root cause unchanged during pretraining. We propose StickyMoE, a differentiable routing consistency loss that penalises abrupt expert switches between adjacent tokens, encouraging the router to maintain the same expert assignment across semantically coherent spans. StickyMoE requires no architectural changes, adds a single hyperparameter lambda, and unlike post-hoc methods, allows expert representations and routing decisions to co-adapt from the first training step. Experiments on small-scale MoE language models show that StickyMoE reduces the expert switch rate by up to 60% with less than 4% perplexity degradation, Pareto-dominating post-hoc fine-tuning on the quality-locality frontier. Routing temporal locality is most efficiently instilled at training time.

</details>


### [125] [Reward Transport: Property Control in Flow Matching via Noise-Space Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08781)
*Kehan Guo,Yili Shen,Yujun Zhou,Yue Huang,Chujie Gao,Shiyi Du,Xiangliang Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种名为Reward Transport的新方法，通过在训练时使用最优传输耦合将噪声空间坐标与分子奖励对齐，实现生成分布的可控调节。该方法在推理阶段仅通过调节一个标量坐标即可实现对分子性质（如logP、QED）的单调控制，且无需奖励模型、梯度引导或额外计算。该接口具有可解释性，能区分不同目标下的结构响应，排除了通用尺寸偏差。同时，该方法与无分类器指导和条件流匹配互补，并揭示了在某些扩散模型中耦合对齐结构缺失的现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有生成模型中的噪声-数据耦合通常被视为计算选择，但本文认为其可作为对齐界面，用于嵌入可控结构。目标是实现无需复杂机制的、连续可调的生成分布控制，尤其在分子生成中实现对特定化学性质的精确调控。

Method: 引入基于最优传输的耦合策略，在训练时将噪声空间中的标量坐标与分子奖励对齐；在推理时通过调节该标量坐标，直接控制生成分子的属性分布。该方法在耦合保持极限下等价于截断的交叉熵方法，提供了一个连续可调的分布控制机制。

Result: 在ZINC-250K和GuacaMol数据集上，通过调节单一标量坐标，实现了logP的单调控制和QED的稳定控制；不同目标下表现出相反的结构响应（如logP增大分子，QED减小分子），证明控制非源于通用尺寸偏好。此外，该方法与现有技术互补，且在epsilon-prediction扩散模型中未观察到耦合对齐，表明其依赖于特定模型结构。

Conclusion: Reward Transport通过将噪声-数据耦合视为可操控的对齐接口，实现了无需奖励模型或梯度引导的高效、连续、可解释的生成控制。该方法为分子生成提供了新的设计范式，具有广泛的应用潜力。

Abstract: The coupling in flow matching -- the rule pairing noise vectors with data points -- is typically treated as a computational choice. We show that this coupling can instead serve as an alignment interface: by matching noise and data according to a target molecular property, it embeds controllable structure directly into the learned flow field. Building on this view, we introduce Reward Transport, which uses optimal transport coupling at training time to align a scalar noise-space coordinate with molecular rewards; at inference, varying this coordinate steers the generated distribution without requiring an oracle, reward model, gradient guidance, or additional computation. In the coupling-preserving limit, thresholding this coordinate recovers the Cross-Entropy Method's truncated reward distribution, providing a principled, continuously adjustable distribution-level control knob. Empirically, on ZINC-250K and GuacaMol, sweeping the scalar induces monotone control of logP and consistent QED control over its operating range; most tellingly, the same knob produces opposite structural responses for different targets, growing molecules for logP but shrinking them for QED, which rules out a generic size bias. The interface is complementary to classifier-free guidance and conditional flow matching, while a negative result under epsilon-prediction diffusion clarifies where coupling-level alignment is structurally absent. Code: https://github.com/KehanGuo2/reward-transport

### [126] [Director: Accelerating Distributed MoE Serving via Online Proactive Expert Placement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08782)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Expert parallelism has become the prevailing paradigm to serve Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) models. Existing works for optimizing expert placement focus on leveraging past requests' expert activation patterns. Implementing such an approach requires addressing several challenges: the uncertainty associated with incoming requests' expert activation, the cost of expert migration, and the NP-hard complexity in optimization. Therefore, we present Director, a new distributed MoE serving system that minimizes end-to-end latency via prediction-driven, online expert placement. Director uses either a lightweight cascaded predictor or a low-bit quantized replica for expert activation patterns of incoming requests. To address these limitations, we propose LieBN, a framework for Riemannian Batch Normalization (RBN) over Lie groups. ### [128] [HERO: A Heterogeneity-Aware Benchmark Library for Federated Continual Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08784)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: HERO通过分离任务划分、客户端数据划分和客户端任务序列三个独立维度，构建可控的基准数据流；引入参数α控制客户端数据偏斜，ρ控制任务顺序不匹配，从而系统化地生成多样化的异质性场景。

Conclusion: HERO为联邦持续学习提供了首个可比较、可解释且可复现的基准框架，其解耦设计有助于深入理解方法在真实异构环境中的鲁棒性与局限性，并推动更透明的评估实践。

Abstract: Federated continual learning (FCL) evaluates how distributed clients learn from changing data streams while retaining previously learned knowledge. Existing evaluations are difficult to compare because they often change datasets, task splits, client data splits, task orders, backbones, memory assumptions, and reporting rules simultaneously. We introduce \textbf{HERO}, a heterogeneity-aware benchmark library for FCL. HERO builds benchmark streams by separating three choices that are often coupled, namely the task split, the client data split, and the client task sequence. In HERO-Core, the main comparable benchmark, $α$ controls client data skew and $ρ$ controls task-order mismatch. We evaluate representative FCL methods on CIFAR-100 and TinyImageNet using final average accuracy, average forgetting, and bottom-10\% client accuracy. We also include a graph-based Domain-IL portability case study on OGB-MolPCBA, where scaffold-domain granularity changes the input distribution while the prediction task remains fixed. Our results show that method behavior changes across easy and heterogeneous settings, that average accuracy can hide weak bottom-client performance, that task-order mismatch favors different strategies from synchronized evaluation, and that the same HERO interface can expose domain-shift difficulty beyond image-based FCIL. HERO releases benchmark streams, configurations, method implementations, and reporting scripts to support reproducible and setting-aware FCL evaluation.

### [130] [Accelerating GPU Inference of Large Language Models with Moderately Unstructured Sparse Weight Matrices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08786)
*Tao Lu,Haoyu Wang,Zonghui Wang,Keshen Xiang,Jiaheng Zhang,Wenzhi Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种针对中等稀疏度大语言模型（LLM）的高效GPU推理方法，通过三层次矩阵存储格式（Sparse-TC、Slot-Filling和Residual层）与专用SpMM内核设计，首次在配备高带宽内存（HBM）的现代GPU上实现稀疏矩阵乘法超越密集矩阵乘法的性能。该方法利用稀疏张量核心与CUDA核心协同计算，优化执行流水线并重叠计算与内存访问，达到最高1.64倍内核级加速和1.41倍端到端加速，优于SpInfer和FlashLLM。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出三层矩阵存储格式：(i) Sparse-TC层，利用稀疏张量核心加速SpMM；(ii) Slot-Filling层，采用并行差分距离压缩矩阵并支持低成本片上解码；(iii) 轻量级Residual层，确保SpMM计算正确性。基于此设计了一种联合使用稀疏张量核心与CUDA核心的SpMM内核，实现高效执行流水线，并重叠片上计算与内存访问。

Result: 实验表明，该方法是首个在现代配备HBM的GPU上实现稀疏矩阵乘法性能超越密集矩阵乘法的工作。相比SpInfer（EuroSys'25最佳论文），内核级别速度提升最高达1.64倍；相比FlashLLM（VLDB'24），端到端推理加速最高达1.41倍。

Conclusion: 本文提出的稀疏存储格式与内核设计有效突破了中等稀疏度下稀疏计算难以超越密集计算的瓶颈，为大语言模型的高效GPU推理提供了新范式，具备显著性能优势和实际部署价值。

Abstract: With the growing deployment of large language models (LLMs), LLM inference cost has become a key challenge. Pruning techniques that introduce sparsity into weight matrices can accelerate inference. However, maintaining model quality typically limits pruning to moderate unstructured sparsity (around 50\%). At these sparsity levels, none of the existing GPU kernels for sparse matrix multiplication (SpMM) can outperform their dense counterparts. This paper proposes an efficient GPU inference method for LLMs with moderate sparsity. We propose a three-layer matrix storage format comprising: (i) a Sparse-TC layer enabling sparse tensor cores to accelerate SpMM; (ii) a Slot-Filling layer using parallel differential distance for matrix compression while supporting low-cost on-chip decoding; (iii) a lightweight Residual Layer ensuring correct SpMM computation. Building on this format, we design a SpMM kernel that jointly utilizes sparse tensor cores and CUDA cores. This design enables an efficient execution pipeline and overlaps on-chip computation with memory access. Evaluations show that our work is the first to outperform dense matrix multiplication on modern GPUs equipped with high-bandwidth memory (HBM). It achieves up to 1.64x kernel-level speedup over SpInfer (EuroSys'25, Best paper) and up to 1.41x end-to-end speedups over FlashLLM (VLDB'24). Our source code: https://github.com/moui0/cudac.

### [131] [Adaptive Bayes exactly tracks information over intrinsic time](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08789)
*Akshay Balsubramani*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了贝叶斯更新与乘法权重更新等方法在序列反馈下的后悔值遵循一个精确的信息会计恒等式。每一轮中，学习者的超额损失可分解为当期对不确定性暴露的即时支付，以及当前权重与参考策略间信息距离的减少。累积支付构成路径相关的不确定性时钟（即“内在时间”），从而导出两种精确的后悔值自适应分解方式。这些分解不依赖于上界，而是直接反映实际路径特性，使得有利的随机或低噪声情形表现为内在时间的自约束性质。该分析框架统一适用于Hedge、乐观更新、侧信息、连续先验、提升算法、在线凸优化、上下文老虎机及重复博弈等多种场景，其路径层面的会计逻辑一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究多通过上界分析后悔值，难以揭示实际路径中的结构性特征。本文旨在建立一种精确的信息会计框架，以揭示不同更新规则下后悔值的本质结构，从而更深刻理解算法在真实序列中的行为表现。

Method: 提出基于信息距离和路径相关不确定性的精确会计恒等式，推导出两种自然的后悔值分解方式；利用信息论工具分析各类算法中的权重更新机制，并证明其共性。

Result: 发现了所有此类更新规则均满足相同的路径级信息会计恒等式；建立了内在时间的概念，并实现后悔值的精确分解；揭示了低噪声或有利环境下的自约束性质源于内在时间的自限行为。

Conclusion: 该信息会计框架提供了一个统一且精确的视角来理解多种在线学习算法的行为，将复杂动态过程简化为可解释的路径相关量——内在时间，为设计高效、鲁棒的在线学习系统提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Bayesian and multiplicative-weights updates reweight experts, models, or actions from sequential feedback. We show that the regret of any such update obeys an exact information-accounting identity. On each round, the learner's excess loss to any chosen comparator is the sum of an immediate payment for the uncertainty exposed by the round and a reduction in the information distance from the learner's current weights to the comparator. The cumulative payment defines a pathwise uncertainty clock, the \emph{intrinsic time} of the realized sequence. Summing one-step balances yields two exact adaptive decompositions of cumulative regret, one for each natural way of composing the update across rounds. Because the decompositions are exact rather than upper bounds, favorable stochastic or low-noise regimes appear as self-bounding properties of the realized intrinsic time, not as slack in worst-case analyses. The same calculus covers Hedge, optimistic and side-information variants, continuous priors, boosting, online convex optimization, contextual bandits, and repeated games: the pathwise account is the same in every case.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准强化学习中的探索方法依赖动作空间的随机性，但此类局部扰动难以突破性能瓶颈；而大型语言模型和视觉-语言-动作模型提供了通过修改自然语言提示实现全局行为改变的可能性，但如何找到有效提示仍是挑战，尤其在初始成功率极低、奖励极度稀疏的情况下。

Method: PDE方法基于视觉语言模型（VLM）分析环境交互的视频回放，识别当前策略的失败原因，并自动重写初始提示以引导下一次尝试。该过程模拟了后验采样机制，使提示分布随经验不断更新，实现对有效提示的渐进式搜索。

Result: 在多种操纵和推理任务中，PDE能够从零奖励起点学习出有效策略，且在样本效率方面优于传统方法，展现出强大的探索能力与泛化潜力。

Conclusion: 提示驱动探索（PDE）为强化学习提供了一种新颖、高效的探索范式，通过将自然语言提示作为可优化的元变量，实现了对策略的全局调控，具有广泛的应用前景。

Abstract: Exploration is essential to RL since a policy cannot improve by repeatedly sampling the behaviors it already prefers. Standard methods inject stochasticity in the action space, but such jitter only yields rollouts close to the original. Escaping a weak policy often requires global perturbations that action noise cannot produce. Large language models (LLMs) and vision-language-action (VLA) models offer a pathway: they condition the policy on a natural language prompt, and since the rollout follows from it, modifying the prompt induces global changes. The challenge is finding prompts that induce useful global changes. With a weak policy that rarely succeeds, reward is too sparse to select on. Our idea is to refine prompts from the rollouts themselves: a vision-language model (VLM) reasons over the rollout video, diagnoses how the policy responded, and rewrites the prompt to elicit better behavior next time. This procedure realizes posterior sampling, a classical RL exploration framework, at the level of prompts: the VLM maintains an implicit distribution over useful prompts and updates it from observed rollouts. We call this strategy Prompt-Driven Exploration (PDE). Across manipulation and reasoning tasks, PDE enables RL to learn successful policies even from zero-reward starts, and improves sample efficiency more broadly. Our website is available at https://xinyunsunshine.github.io/prompt-rl.

</details>


### [133] [How are linear representations learned? Exact solutions to the dynamics of abstraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08843)
*William W. Yang,Andrew M. Saxe,Peter E. Latham*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了在训练过程中概念方向如何在神经网络表示空间中逐渐形成，这一过程称为“抽象”。在最小线性网络设置下，作者得到了抽象轨迹的精确解，揭示了数据与目标几何结构共同决定最终抽象程度、网络深度促进抽象、初始化规模控制训练中最大抽象度等关键原理。扩展到非线性网络后发现，erf网络近似线性理论，而ReLU网络的抽象更依赖输入几何而非目标几何；且无论哪种非线性，激活值的抽象程度均弱于预激活值，存在一种“衰减定律”。该理论在DINOv3和Gemma 4等开放模型中得到验证，并可用于提升大语言模型中线性探针的泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解神经网络在训练过程中如何逐步形成可解释的概念方向（即抽象过程），以支持更有效的可解释性和控制方法。现有研究多关注训练后的抽象状态，但对训练动态机制缺乏深入理解。

Method: 构建分析抽象过程的理论框架，在最小线性网络中推导出抽象轨迹的精确解；通过引入非线性（如erf、ReLU）扩展理论，分析其对抽象动力学的影响；提出并验证“衰减定律”——非线性导致激活层抽象弱于预激活层；在真实模型中进行实证检验并应用于改进线性探针性能。

Result: 发现了抽象的三大解析原则：1）最终抽象由数据与目标几何共同决定；2）网络越深，抽象越强；3）初始化尺度限制最大抽象程度。非线性网络中，抽象受输入几何影响更大，且普遍存在从预激活到激活的抽象衰减现象。在DINOv3和Gemma 4中观察到该衰减规律，且基于理论的改进显著提升了线性探针的泛化能力。

Conclusion: 本文建立了关于神经网络中抽象过程的动力学理论，揭示了从训练初期到后期概念方向形成的内在机制，为解释性方法和激活控制提供了理论基础与实践指导。

Abstract: In artificial and biological neural networks, concepts are often encoded as consistent linear directions in representation space. In deep learning, this idea is known as the linear representation hypothesis and underpins many interpretability and control methods based on linear probes, from concept detection to activation steering. Yet while prior work has studied whether such directions should exist $\textit{after}$ training, the dynamics of how they emerge $\textit{during}$ training remain poorly understood. Here, we develop a framework to study the alignment of concept directions during training - a process we call "abstraction". In a minimal linear network setting, we obtain exact solutions for the full trajectory of abstraction. These solutions reveal key analytic principles governing abstraction: (i) data and target geometry jointly determine abstraction at the end-of-learning, (ii) abstraction improves with network depth, and (iii) initialization scale controls the maximum abstraction reached during training. Extending our theory to nonlinear networks, we analyze how the choice of nonlinearity affects abstraction dynamics: erf networks approximate the linear theory, while abstraction in ReLU networks depends less on target geometry and more on input geometry. Across both, we prove a striking attenuation law: both nonlinearities weaken abstraction in activations relative to preactivations. We find evidence for this law in open models (DINOv3, Gemma 4) and apply our theory to improve linear probe generalization in LLMs. Together, our results provide a dynamical theory of abstraction with implications for interpretability and control.

</details>


### [134] [Optimizing Against Safety Representations: Activation-Guided Adversarial Suffixes and the Geometry of Refusal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08883)
*Ege Çakar,Hannah Guan,Kayden Kehe*

TL;DR: 本文研究大语言模型中安全表示的分布特性，通过对抗性后缀攻击作为探针，提出Activation-Guided GCG和Soft-GCG方法，发现安全拒绝行为由全层、全位置的分布式表示支持，而非局部单一位置。较小模型易受攻击，较大模型更具鲁棒性，表明模型规模与安全训练质量影响抗攻击能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型的安全机制可能依赖于脆弱的内部表示，且拒绝行为可能由激活空间中的低维方向驱动。理解这些表示的结构、定位与可优化性对提升模型安全性至关重要。

Method: 引入Activation-Guided GCG，以内部拒绝方向为目标设计损失函数，替代传统输出级目标；提出Soft-GCG，采用Gumbel-Softmax实现连续松弛，加速搜索过程。

Result: 全局抑制所有层和位置的拒绝方向比局部攻击更有效；Soft-GCG实现33倍加速并提升攻击成功率；小模型易被攻破，大模型在计算受限条件下表现出更强的抗攻击能力。

Conclusion: 安全机制在模型中是分布式的，而非集中于某一点；该发现为设计更鲁棒、基于表示的对齐策略提供了实证依据。

Abstract: Behavioral alignment in large language models often masks fragile internal safety representations. Recent work suggests that refusal behavior is mediated by low-dimensional directions in activation space. This raises questions about how such representations are structured, localized, and accessed by optimization. We study adversarial suffix attacks as a probe of representational alignment. We introduce Activation-Guided GCG, which replaces output-based objectives with losses that directly target a model's internal refusal direction. Across several objective variants, we find that suppressing refusal globally across all layers and positions is more effective than targeting a single layer-position pair. This suggests that safety representations are distributed across the forward pass rather than causally localized to a single site. We further introduce Soft-GCG, a continuous relaxation of discrete suffix optimization using Gumbel-Softmax. Soft-GCG achieves a 33 $\times$ speedup over standard GCG while improving attack success rates. Evaluating across model scales, we find that smaller models remain vulnerable while larger models resist both activation- and suffix-based attacks at our compute-constrained settings, consistent with larger and better safety trained models being harder to jailbreak. Together, our results clarify how safety mechanisms are encoded and can be broken in contemporary models. These insights provide concrete guidance for designing more robust and representation-aware alignment strategies.

*Minett Tran,Taehee Jeong*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种模式感知的图神经网络，显式编码缺失特征的信息，以利用缺失模式中的潜在信息。在七个具有自然缺失数据的UCI数据集上，该方法在平衡准确率和F1宏平均上分别实现了17%和22%的平均提升。简单随机模式嵌入表现接近于学习嵌入，表明区分缺失模式比任务特定优化更重要。注意力机制虽有帮助，但在模式信息可用时并非必需。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出模式感知的图神经网络，通过四种编码策略（学习嵌入、固定随机嵌入、统计特征、层次表示）显式建模缺失模式，并在图神经网络中融合这些信息。

Conclusion: 缺失模式可提供重要信息，显式建模缺失模式能显著提升模型性能；即使简单的随机嵌入也表现良好，说明模式区分比精细化优化更为关键；注意力机制在模式信息存在时作用有限。

Abstract: Missing data is ubiquitous in real-world datasets. Traditional methods either discard incomplete samples or apply imputation techniques that ignore potentially informative missingness patterns, implicitly assuming that missingness occurs randomly. However, missingness patterns might provide additional information. We propose pattern-aware graph neural networks that explicitly encode which features are missing alongside observed values. We used four encoding strategies -- learned embeddings, frozen random embeddings, statistical features, and hierarchical representations -- across seven UCI datasets with naturally occurring missingness. Our Pattern-aware methods achieve substantial improvements over baselines, with an average improvement of 17\% in balanced accuracy and 22\% in F1-macro across all datasets. The benefits vary significantly by dataset: annealing shows dramatic improvement (+80\% balanced accuracy), while hepatitis and soybean show minimal gains (+4--5\%). Notably, even simple random pattern embeddings perform comparably to learned embeddings (0.650 vs 0.663 balanced accuracy), suggesting that distinguishing between patterns may be more important than task-specific optimization. Our ablation study reveals that attention mechanisms, while helpful, are not critical when pattern information is available -- simple mean aggregation with pattern awareness achieves 0.640 balanced accuracy compared to 0.645 for attention-based variants.

### [136] [A Machine Learning Surrogate for Component Criticality Ranking in Interdependent Power-Communication Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08918)
*Sohini Roy,Xheni Hylviu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于梯度提升的机器学习代理模型，用于高效预测电力-通信耦合系统中大规模N-k故障场景下的严重程度和组件关键性排名。该模型利用无泄漏的结构特征，在IEEE 118节点系统上实现了0.849的置信度相关性（严重度预测）和0.853的关键性排序相关性，性能接近基于MIIM真实模拟的上限。结果表明，跨层依赖信息是模型优势的主要来源，且拓扑中心性仅提供较弱基线（0.60–0.69）。研究支持两阶段工作流：先用代理模型快速筛选高风险组件，再对少数关键情形用高保真仿真验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于已发布的修正暗示依赖模型（MIIM）作为真实故障传播模拟器，构建一个机器学习代理模型，使用无泄漏的结构特征进行训练，通过梯度提升算法预测每种故障情景的严重程度，并推导出组件关键性排名。

Conclusion: 所提出的机器学习代理模型能高效、准确地评估复杂耦合系统的故障严重性与组件关键性，显著降低计算负担。结合高保真仿真，可形成高效的两阶段韧性分析流程，适用于实际电网规划中的优先级加固决策。

Abstract: Cyber-physical power systems are vulnerable to cascading failures caused by tight interdependencies between power and communication infrastructures. Evaluating these failures over large N-k contingency sets with a high-fidelity simulator is computationally prohibitive for resilience planning. Using the previously published Modified Implicative Interdependency Model (MIIM) as the ground-truth cascade simulator, this paper develops a machine-learning surrogate that predicts contingency severity from leakage-free structural features and derives a component-criticality ranking for prioritized hardening analysis. On the IEEE 118-bus system, the Gradient Boosting surrogate achieves Spearman correlations of 0.849 for per-contingency severity prediction and 0.853 for per-component criticality ranking, while remaining stable across three independently sampled datasets. MIIM-derived component criticality itself reproduces only to a Spearman of approximately 0.85 under the present sampling pipeline, and the surrogate operates at this empirical ceiling to within sampling variation. Topological centrality measures on the full interdependent network provide meaningful baselines (Spearman 0.60-0.69), and feature ablation shows that the surrogate's advantage is driven primarily by inter-layer dependency information. These results support a two-stage workflow in which the surrogate rapidly ranks candidate components and MIIM is reserved for selective verification.

### [137] [SafeExplorer: An Unbiased Policy Gradient for Reinforcement Learning with Recovery Interventions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08925)
*Elham Daneshmand,Majid Khadiv,Glen Berseth,Hsiu-Chin Lin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究提出一种改进的PPO算法，用于在物理机器人上训练强化学习代理时最小化跌倒次数。通过引入无偏策略梯度估计器，仅在安全时间步使用得分函数，避免了恢复策略确定性导致的重要性采样失效问题。此外，结合闭式价值函数和模仿损失，显著加速学习并减少跌倒，实验显示在HalfCheetah、Ant、Unitree Go1上跌倒次数分别减少233倍、48倍、26倍，同时保持或超越标准PPO的最终奖励表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在物理机器人上训练强化学习代理时，每次跌倒都可能导致硬件损坏且无法像模拟器那样重置，因此必须最小化跌倒次数，而传统方法如约束MDP将跌倒与回报权衡，不适用于此场景。现有方法依赖恢复策略处理脱离安全区域的情况，但会引入策略更新偏差，且当恢复策略为确定性时，重要性采样无法定义，导致无法有效修正偏差。

Method: 提出一种无需修改即可集成到PPO中的新方法：1）设计一个仅在安全时间步使用得分函数的无偏策略梯度估计器，避免评估恢复策略密度；2）在确定性动力学和恢复策略下，提供恢复触发状态的闭式值函数；3）引入模仿损失，仅在恢复成功时复制恢复动作，以加速学习。

Result: 在三个环境（HalfCheetah、Ant、Unitree Go1）五个种子的基准测试中，该方法将训练期间跌倒次数分别减少了233倍、48倍、26倍，同时达到或超过标准PPO的最终奖励；在恢复策略不可靠的Ant环境中，是唯一能达成最佳奖励80%的方法。

Conclusion: 所提方法有效解决了物理机器人训练中因恢复策略导致的策略更新偏差问题，即使在恢复策略确定性情况下仍保持有效性，显著减少跌倒次数并提升学习效率，具备实际部署潜力。

Abstract: Training reinforcement-learning agents directly on physical robots makes every fall costly, since a fall can damage the platform and cannot be undone like a simulator reset; the goal is therefore to minimize falls during training rather than trade them off against return, as constrained Markov decision process (MDP) formulations do. A standard mitigation hands control to a separate recovery policy whenever the agent leaves a designer-specified safe region (a subset of state space it should stay within), but the resulting mixed-policy rollouts silently bias every on-policy update, and the importance-sampling correction that would remove this bias is ill-defined whenever the recovery policy is deterministic. We address this bias with a drop-in modification of proximal policy optimization (PPO). Its core is an unbiased policy-gradient estimator that uses the score function only at safe timesteps and never evaluates the recovery policy's density, so it stays valid even when the recovery policy is deterministic, exactly where importance sampling breaks, and it empirically dominates importance sampling even when the recovery policy is stochastic. Because the recovery policy still makes credit assignment slow near the safe-region boundary, two further components accelerate learning: a closed-form value for recovery-triggering states when dynamics and recovery are deterministic, and an imitation loss that copies recovery actions only when recovery succeeds. On a three-environment, five-seed benchmark, the resulting algorithm reduces training-time falls by factors of 233x, 48x, and 26x on HalfCheetah, Ant, and Unitree Go1 over standard PPO, while matching or exceeding PPO's final reward, and on Ant, where the recovery policy is unreliable, it is the only method that reaches 80% of the best final reward.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Efficient serving of diffusion large language models (dLLMs) is hindered by convergence heterogeneity: when batching multiple requests, different sequences converge at different rates, causing faster requests to stall behind slower stragglers and introducing compute bubbles and tail latency. We present BlockServe, a continuous batching framework that integrates block-grained scheduling -- immediately evicting completed requests at block boundaries -- with mixed-state execution that extends dual cache and parallel decoding to heterogeneous batches via gather-scatter indexing. Furthermore, a compute-aware admission controller expands effective batch capacity through token-budgeted refill. On Dream and LLaDA across five benchmarks, BlockServe achieves 1.9--10.6$\times$ throughput over Fast-dLLM with comparable generation quality, establishing block-grained scheduling as a foundation for high-throughput offline dLLM inference.

### [139] [TSRouter: Dynamic Modality-Model Selection for Time Series Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08940)
*Fangxu Yu,Tao Feng,Dehai Min,Lu Cheng,Ge Liu,Tianyi Zhou*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: TSRouter 是一个基于图的动态路由框架，用于在时间序列推理中智能选择最适合的模态和模型。它通过构建包含任务、查询、模态和模型节点的异构图，建模它们之间的复杂交互关系，并根据用户定义的性能-成本偏好对模态-模型组合进行评分，从而实现最优路由。该方法在4个不同时间序列推理任务上显著优于基线方法，提升达16\%至46\%，并具备良好的零样本泛化能力与计算效率优化。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在4个不同的时间序列推理任务上，TSRouter相比基线有16\%到46\%的相对性能提升；具有强零样本泛化能力，支持未见模型与新任务的即插即用；同时通过成本感知优化降低计算开销，保持高性能。

Conclusion: TSRouter通过图结构建模与动态路由策略，有效融合多模态优势，在时间序列推理中实现了性能与效率的双重突破，为复杂任务下的智能模型选择提供了可扩展的解决方案。

Abstract: Time series reasoning is essential for real-world problem-solving. While both Large Language Models (LLMs) and Vision-Language Models (VLMs) can reason about time-series data, their capabilities are complementary: LLMs process time series as text sequences and thus preserve exact numerical understanding, but struggle with global patterns, whereas VLMs efficiently capture these patterns by visualizing time series but may lose fine-grained details. Moreover, models vary significantly in task-specific expertise and inference costs. Dynamically selecting the most suitable modality and model for each query is therefore crucial, yet challenging because it requires modeling the complex interactions among tasks, queries, modalities, and models, which carry rich contextual signals. To this end, we introduce TSRouter, a graph-based dynamic routing framework. TSRouter constructs a heterogeneous graph of task, query, modality, and model nodes to contextualize the interactions among query characteristics, modality attributes, and model capabilities. TSRouter formulates routing as a candidate scoring problem, where each modality-model pair is evaluated based on user-defined performance-cost preferences to select the optimal candidate. Comprehensive evaluations on 4 distinct time series reasoning tasks reveal that TSRouter substantially outperforms diverse baselines with 16\% to 46\% relative improvements. Furthermore, TSRouter demonstrates robust zero-shot plug-and-play generalization to unseen models and novel tasks and preserves high performance while reducing computational overhead through cost-aware optimization. Our code is available at https://github.com/tianyi-lab/TSRouter.

</details>


### [140] [Training, Reading, and Editing Legible Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08946)
*Mark Oskin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出通过引入可读性约束（crispness penalty）与通道级方差下限，构建更可解释的Transformer模型。该方法使模型中的操作符从模糊集合运算变为清晰、上下文相关的检测器，显著提升模型可读性：78%的前馈操作符和50%的注意力值通道为清晰检测器，深层网络中每头可读性达78%。同时，模型自动学习单位分配，87%的关键计算由清晰操作完成，且编辑局部性提升50-184倍。通过单元间去相关机制，实现概念解耦，使预测可被简明解释，且性能与传统模型持平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Transformer模型内部操作难以解读，缺乏清晰、可命名的语义单元；尽管已有工作尝试引入分段GELU等结构，但依赖人工设定，灵活性不足。本文旨在构建真正可读的模型，让每个单元具有明确语义功能，并支持精准编辑与解释。

Method: 设计一种基于方差最小化的脆性惩罚机制，结合每通道方差下限以防止操作符退化为常数；引入可学习的单位比例参数替代固定划分；采用层间旋转框架分离检测与命名任务；施加单元间去相关压力以增强独立性。所有目标均以损失函数形式融入训练过程。

Result: 模型在保持与基线相当性能的前提下，实现了前所未有的可读性：深层模块中每头可读性达78%，78%前馈操作符为清晰检测器，50%注意力通道为上下文敏感检测器；编辑范围缩小50-184倍，支持对逻辑合取等复杂概念进行局部修改；预测结果可被少数命名操作直接解释。

Conclusion: 通过合理设计损失函数与训练机制，可以有效引导Transformer内部结构向清晰、可读、可编辑的方向演化，实现高质量与高可解释性的统一，为可解释人工智能提供了新范式。

Abstract: A transformer can be built from operators that are legible by construction -- bounded, named units that read as fuzzy set operations rather than dense activations -- but legibility must be pressed for during training, and the pressure has a failure mode. A crispness penalty meant to sharpen a bounded operator into a decisive detector instead collapses it into a dead constant. An identity, E[v(1-v)] = mu(1-mu) - var, shows why -- the penalty is a variance-minimizer blind to the difference between a live detector and a constant -- and names the fix: a per-channel variance floor, the target legibility metric written as a loss, which recovers both legibility and quality. A learned per-unit fraction then retires the hand-set reserved-GELU partition of prior work: given the choice the model keeps no unit as pure GELU and routes 87% of its load-bearing computation through crisp operators. The result is the most legible transformer we have built -- 78% of its feed-forward operands and 50% of its attention value channels are crisp-and-contextual detectors, and per-head legibility rises from 18% in shallow layers to 78% in deep ones. Read in the correct rotated per-layer frame, these units separate a clean detection (what a unit responds to) from a harder naming (what its output decodes to); and because the objective makes each unit crisp and sparse, edits to them are far more local -- 50-184x in the deep layers where the edit sites concentrate -- and can target explicit conjunctions a single neuron cannot express. Finally, a between-unit decorrelation pressure exposes a legibility dial: it trades a circuit's reuse for independence at no quality cost, turning concepts into single, surgically editable units and a prediction into a short explanation read off a handful of named operations. Quality holds at parity with a conventional baseline throughout.

### [141] [FairSelect: A Systematic Evaluation of Multi-Level and Intersectional Algorithmic Fairness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08953)
*Nick Souligne,Isabella Mixton-Garcia,Vignesh Subbian*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: FairSelect is a toolkit for systematically evaluating fairness mitigation strategies across preprocessing, inprocessing, and postprocessing stages, supporting intersectional subgroup analysis and multi-method combinations. It was validated on synthetic clinical data and a real-world stroke risk prediction task, showing that combined fairness methods often improve fairness with modest performance tradeoffs, though effects are context-dependent and nonadditive.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing fairness methods are typically evaluated in isolation and along single demographic axes, limiting practical guidance for selecting effective strategies in complex, real-world scenarios involving intersectional subgroups and multiple modeling stages.

Method: FairSelect enables systematic evaluation of fairness mitigation strategies across different stages of the modeling lifecycle (preprocessing, inprocessing, postprocessing), supports multiple model architectures, and allows comparison of fairness and utility tradeoffs across baseline, single-method, and multi-level configurations.

Result: Synthetic experiments showed targeted fairness methods reduced subgroup disparities, while combined strategies yielded larger average fairness improvements with small utility costs. In a real-world stroke risk prediction task, some method combinations improved both fairness and performance, while others were ineffective or harmful, highlighting nonadditive and context-dependent interactions.

Conclusion: Fairness interventions interact in complex, nonadditive ways depending on context. FairSelect provides a practical framework to identify effective fairness strategies that enhance subgroup equity without sacrificing model performance in clinical machine learning.

Abstract: Algorithmic fairness methods are increasingly used to identify and mitigate bias in machine learning models, yet most approaches are evaluated in isolation and along single demographic axes. This limits practical guidance for selecting fairness strategies, where disparities may arise across intersectional subgroups and across multiple stages of the modeling lifecycle. This work presents FairSelect, a toolkit for systematically evaluating fairness mitigation strategies applied individually and in combination across preprocessing, inprocessing, and postprocessing stages. FairSelect supports multiple model architectures, intersectional subgroup evaluation, and comparison of fairness utility tradeoffs across baseline, single method, and multi level configurations. The framework was validated using synthetic clinical datasets designed to represent specific bias mechanisms and a real-world replication of two-year stroke risk prediction among patients with atrial fibrillation. Synthetic experiments showed that targeted fairness methods generally reduced intended subgroup disparities, while combined strategies produced larger average fairness improvements with modest utility tradeoffs. In the clinical prediction task, mitigation effects were highly variable, with some combinations improving both fairness and predictive performance while others were ineffective or counterproductive. These findings demonstrate that fairness interventions interact in nonadditive and context dependent ways. FairSelect provides a practical framework for systematically identifying fairness strategies that improve subgroup equity while preserving model performance in clinical machine learning.

### [142] [Eluna: An Agentic LLM System for Automating Warehouse Operations with Reasoning and Task Execution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08960)
*Ning Liu,Kalle Kujanpää,Zhaoxuan Zhu,P Aditya Sreekar,Kaiwen Liu,Chuanneng Sun,Jorge Marchena Menendez,Matthew Bales,Tianyu Yang,Shahnawaz Alam,Rose Yu,Baoyuan Liu,Kristina Klinkner,Shervin Malmasi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Eluna 是一个用于可靠执行标准操作流程（SOP）的生产级代理系统，采用图引导的多代理架构，将 SOP 编码为有向无环图并逐步披露任务，通过并行子代理实现独立任务处理。为满足生产环境中的延迟与准确率要求，引入非对称情景蒸馏机制：强教师模型通过情景错误记忆持续改进，再由小型学生模型在去除记忆的修正轨迹上微调，从而内化纠错能力且无需推理时开销。在13个任务基准和两个实际应用中，优化后的模型性能达到或超过教师模型，优于所有更大的现成基线，并在票务处理任务中实现94%专家一致率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM 代理在执行复杂、多系统决策逻辑的 SOP 时缺乏程序合规性保障机制，且在面对完整 SOP 规范带来的上下文过载时性能下降，亟需一种可信赖、高效、符合生产要求的 SOP 执行框架。

Method: Eluna 采用图引导的多代理架构，将 SOP 编码为有向无环图，实现任务的渐进式披露；并行子代理具备持久代码执行与实时数据访问能力；采用非对称情景蒸馏策略，利用教师模型的错误记忆进行迭代优化，再通过学生模型在无记忆条件下微调，实现高效知识迁移与推理加速。

Result: 在13项任务基准测试及两项真实生产应用中，经过微调的 Eluna 模型在准确率和响应速度上均达到或超越其教师模型，显著优于所有更大规模的现成基线模型，在票务处理任务中达成94%的专家一致性水平。

Conclusion: Eluna 成功构建了一个可部署于生产环境的高可靠性 SOP 执行系统，通过图结构引导与非对称蒸馏机制有效解决了 LLM 代理在复杂流程执行中的合规性与上下文过载问题，为工业级智能代理系统提供了可扩展、高效、精准的新范式。

Abstract: Warehouse operations are governed by Standard Operating Procedures (SOPs) that encode complex, multi-system decision logic, which must be executed reliably under strict time constraints, yet LLM agents lack mechanisms to enforce procedural compliance and degrade under the context overload full SOP specifications introduce. We present Eluna, a production-deployed agentic system for reliable SOP execution. Eluna is a graph-guided, multi-agent framework that encodes SOPs as directed acyclic graphs with progressive disclosure and delegates independent tasks to parallel sub-agents, each with persistent code execution and live data access. To meet production latency and accuracy needs, we use asymmetric episodic distillation where a strong teacher is improved through episodic error memories, then a smaller student is fine-tuned on the corrected trajectories with memory stripped, internalizing corrections without inference-time overhead. On a 13-task benchmark and two production applications, our fine-tuned models match or exceed their teacher, beat all larger off-the-shelf baselines, and reach 94% expert agreement on the ticket processing application.

### [143] [NL-PAC: Specification Ambiguity and Certified Minimax Risk Floors in LLM-Mediated Supervision](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08961)
*Berkay Anahtarci*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出NL-PAC框架，利用固定模型的阈值解码规则定义可接受标签和候选目标。在目标不可知监督下，任何学习者在每种样本规模下都会面临至少一半直径的最坏情况风险；最小最大风险由数据无关策略精确实现。有限样本置信区间使这些量可从保留的未标记输入中验证。在冻结的Qwen 2.5-3B审计中，一个预设提示产生正的模型相对证书，而改写和精确规则对照组则为零。保留桥审计发现，提供的候选阅读条款不满足传递证书所需的可接受性条件。该保证特定于被审计模型、提示、阈值和输入分布；扩展到人类解释需外部验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当自然语言任务规范存在多种解读但监督通道无法揭示实际采用的解读时，额外标签虽减少采样误差，却无法解决识别问题。因此需要一种能形式化可接受标签与候选目标的方法，并提供可验证的风险保障。

Method: 引入NL-PAC框架，基于固定模型的阈值解码规则定义点态可接受的目标类；通过分析该类直径，推导出在目标盲监督下的最坏情况风险下界；使用有限样本置信区间对风险和可接受性进行可验证评估；并通过实证审计验证框架有效性。

Result: 在冻结的Qwen 2.5-3B模型上，一个预设提示获得正的模型相对证书，而其他控制条件（改写和精确规则）未获得；桥审计显示候选阅读条款不满足可接受性条件，无法转移证书；证明该保证依赖于具体模型、提示、阈值与输入分布，不能直接推广至人类解释。

Conclusion: NL-PAC提供了一种在自然语言规范存在歧义时，形式化可接受标签并量化风险的可验证框架。其保证具有高度特异性，仅适用于特定模型、提示和输入分布，扩展至人类解释需依赖外部验证。

Abstract: Large language models increasingly provide labels, evaluations, and feedback for tasks specified in natural language. When a specification admits multiple readings but the supervision channel does not reveal which is operative, additional labels reduce sampling error without resolving the resulting identification problem. We introduce Natural Language PAC (NL-PAC), a framework that uses a fixed model's thresholded decoding law to define admissible labels and candidate targets. The probability that multiple labels are admissible equals the diameter of the pointwise-admissible target class, and under target-blind supervision every learner incurs worst-case risk of at least half this diameter, at every sample size; the exact randomized minimax risk over this class is attained by a data-independent strategy. Finite-sample confidence bounds make these quantities certifiable from held-out unlabeled inputs. In a frozen Qwen~2.5--3B audit, one prespecified prompt yields a positive model-relative certificate, whereas a paraphrase and exact-rule controls yield zero. A held-out bridge audit finds that supplied candidate reading clauses fail the admissibility condition needed to transfer the certificate to coherent readings. The guarantee is specific to the audited model, prompt, threshold, and input distribution; extending it to human interpretations requires external validation.

### [144] [Stochastic Linear Bandits with Partially Observed Actions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08971)
*Gautam Dasarathy,Vineet Gattani,Lalit Jain*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了部分可观测的随机线性贝叶斯问题，其中学习者只能观测到动作向量的随机子集。针对此类问题，作者提出TOFU-POV算法，通过估计潜在动作子空间、使用分段冻结表示进行动作补全，并在低维坐标中运行OFUL，实现了与内在维度相关的$\sqrt{T}$级后悔率。该算法不依赖于环境维度，且可适应未知的内在维度。理论分析揭示了缺失性、决策集大小和子空间条件之间的权衡关系，并提出了一个基于新型乘积构造的下界证明。实验结果支持理论分析，表明算法在合成与真实数据上均显著优于基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在推荐系统和医疗等场景中，完整动作描述可能成本高昂或不可行，导致仅能观测动作向量的部分坐标。传统方法在此类部分可观测设置下难以实现亚线性后悔，因此需要新的算法与理论框架来克服信息瓶颈。

Method: 提出TOFU-POV算法：利用掩码动作估计潜在子空间；采用分段冻结的表示进行当前动作的补全；在低维子空间中运行OFUL算法。此外设计了无需预先知道内在维度的自适应版本。

Result: TOFU-POV实现了与内在子空间维度相关的$\sqrt{T}$后悔率，而非环境维度。理论揭示了缺失性、决策集大小和子空间条件之间的交互作用。下界分析表明，部分观测引入了固有的额外成本。实验验证了算法在合成与真实数据上的优越性能。

Conclusion: 当动作向量具有低内在维度时，即使在部分可观测条件下，仍可实现亚线性后悔。提出的算法有效克服了信息瓶颈，为高维但低秩的动作空间提供了高效学习方案。

Abstract: The stochastic linear bandit, where actions are represented as vectors and rewards are linear, is a central paradigm for sequential decision making. We study a partially observed variant of this problem in which the learning agent only sees a random subset of coordinates for each action. Such partial observability arises naturally in settings like recommendation and healthcare, where full action descriptions can be expensive or even impossible to obtain. In general, this makes sublinear regret information-theoretically impossible. However, we show that this barrier can be overcome when the action vectors have low intrinsic dimension. We propose an algorithm, TOFU-POV, that estimates the latent action subspace using the masked actions, imputes current actions using an epoch-wise frozen representation, and runs OFUL in the resulting low-dimensional coordinates. Our theory shows that TOFU-POV enjoys a $\sqrt{T}$ regret that scales with the intrinsic action subspace dimension as opposed to the ambient dimension and quantifies the interaction between these quantities and the missingness, decision set size, and subspace conditioning. We also devise a rank-adaptive algorithm that does not require the knowledge of the intrinsic dimension. We complement these guarantees with a lower bound based on a novel product construction that separates usual reward-learning uncertainty from a missingness-dependent cost intrinsic to partial observation. Synthetic and real data experiments support our theory and show that TOFU-POV can substantially improve upon natural baselines in this challenging problem.

### [145] [Federated Low-Rank Koopman Learning for Multivariate Time-Series Anomaly Detection in IoT Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08978)
*Tung-Anh Nguyen,Van-Phuc Bui,Anh Tuyen Le,Kim Hue Ta,Minh Thuy Le,J. Andrew Zhang,Xiaojing Huang*

Method: 提出FedKAD框架，采用滑动窗口构建轻量级科波曼表示以捕捉正常时序动态；将联邦训练形式化为低秩共识问题，仅交换紧凑的子空间变量；设计联邦Stiefel-ADMM算法优化共享表示，并在部分客户端参与下进行收敛性与站位性分析；推理阶段通过本地计算预测残差实现异常检测。

Result: 在四个主流多变量时间序列异常检测基准上，FedKAD在检测性能上与联邦深度学习基线相当或更优；训练速度提升2.1×10³倍，通信开销降低80倍，推理延迟降低79倍，充分验证其在资源受限边缘设备上的适用性。

Conclusion: FedKAD是一种高效、轻量、适合边缘部署的联邦异常检测框架，通过科波曼表示与低秩联邦优化，在保证检测性能的同时大幅降低资源消耗，是面向分布式物联网系统中异常检测的理想解决方案。

Abstract: Distributed IoT systems generate multivariate time-series streams for monitoring physical assets, servers, and embedded sensing platforms. Detecting abnormal temporal behavior is critical for fault diagnosis, predictive maintenance, and security. However, practical IoT anomaly detection is hindered by decentralized and non-IID data, limited bandwidth, and the constrained computation and memory of edge devices. This paper proposes FedKAD, a resource-efficient federated Koopman anomaly detection framework for distributed IoT multivariate time series. Unlike deep-learning-based anomaly detectors that require training and communicating large neural models, FedKAD learns normal temporal dynamics through lightweight sliding-window Koopman representations. Federated training is formulated as a low-rank consensus problem, where raw sensor streams and local reduced dynamics remain on device while only compact subspace variables are exchanged with the server. To optimize the shared representation under orthonormality constraints, we develop a federated Stiefel-ADMM algorithm and provide convergence and stationarity analysis under partial client participation. During inference, each client detects anomalies locally by measuring the prediction residual between observed future trajectories and the learned Koopman dynamics. Experiments on four widely used multivariate time-series anomaly detection benchmarks show that FedKAD maintains or improves detection performance compared with federated deep-learning baselines. More importantly for IoT deployment, FedKAD provides up to $2.1\times10^3$ faster training, $80\times$ lower communication, and $79\times$ lower inference latency than neural baselines, confirming its suitability for resource-constrained edge devices.

### [146] [Optimal Top-$k$ Identification from Pairwise Comparisons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08979)
*Motti Goldberger,Nils Rudi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了从噪声成对比较中进行固定置信度top-k识别的主动学习问题。提出了一种渐近最优的算法，通过将下界结构化为鞍点问题，并设计了一个计算高效的原-对偶过程来在线学习最优比较分配，进而构建一个自适应的比较分配算法，证明其具有渐近最优性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在已有的固定置信度纯探索问题中，尽管已有多种渐近最优算法，但针对基于潜在效用模型的成对比较中top-k识别问题，尚无渐近最优算法被建立。因此，本文旨在填补这一空白，设计出一种能够最小化期望比较次数（样本复杂度）且在δ趋近于0时达到信息论下界的算法。

Method: 通过分析问题的下界结构，将其形式化为一个鞍点问题；利用该结构设计一个计算高效的原-对偶算法以在线学习最优比较分配；进一步构造一个自适应的比较分配算法，使其跟踪原-对偶过程的学习结果。

Result: 提出并证明了所设计的自适应比较分配算法在δ→0时具有渐近最优性，即其期望样本复杂度逼近信息论下界。

Conclusion: 本文首次为基于潜在效用模型的成对比较中的top-k识别问题提供了渐近最优的主动学习算法，通过原-对偶方法实现了高效且最优的比较分配策略。

Abstract: We study the active learning problem of fixed-confidence top-$k$ identification from noisy pairwise comparisons. In this problem, an algorithm sequentially chooses pairs of items to compare, observes the outcomes, and stops when it can return the set of top-$k$ items with error probability at most $δ$. The objective is to design such a $δ$-correct procedure that minimizes the expected number of comparisons (the sample complexity). This problem falls within the broader literature on fixed-confidence pure exploration in bandit models, where a common target is asymptotic optimality: the algorithm's expected sample complexity matches the information theoretic lower bound as $δ\to 0$. Asymptotically optimal procedures have been developed for a range of fixed-confidence pure-exploration problems, however to the best of our knowledge, for top-$1$, or more generally top-$k$ identification from pairwise comparisons under latent utility models an asymptotically optimal algorithm has not been established. In this setting, we develop such an algorithm. We characterize the structure of the lower bound and formulate it as a saddle-point problem. This structure enables a computationally efficient primal-dual procedure that learns the asymptotically optimal comparison allocation online. We then construct an adaptive comparison-allocation algorithm that tracks the allocation learned by the primal-dual procedure and prove it is asymptotically optimal.

</details>


### [147] [AlphaZero in Sparsely Rewarded Games: Limits and Auxiliary Supervision](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08984)
*Brent Kong,Tejas Ram,Tony Yue Yu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: AlphaZero achieves strong but not perfect play in Connect Four and Chomp. AZAL, with oracle-derived policy supervision, significantly improves consistency with optimal play, especially in Chomp, though perfect play is not fully achieved in all cases.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To investigate the gap between strong and perfect play in AlphaZero, particularly in domains with known optimal strategies (Connect Four and Chomp), and to evaluate whether architectural or training modifications can close this gap.

Method: A unified self-play + MCTS pipeline is used across both games. Variants include vanilla AlphaZero, a multi-frame input version (limited to Chomp), and AlphaZero Auxiliary Loss (AZAL) that incorporates oracle-derived policy signals. Performance is evaluated via oracle consistency on full-game traces and sampled states.

Result: Vanilla AlphaZero shows strong performance but fails to maintain exact optimal trajectories: it deviates from optimal lines in Connect Four and cannot consistently preserve the g=0 invariant in Chomp. Multi-frame inputs alone do not eliminate the gap in Chomp. AZAL significantly improves oracle consistency—achieving perfect consistency on 10x11 Chomp boards and high consistency on 9x10; in Connect Four, it improves match rates and delays errors but does not reach perfect play.

Conclusion: While AlphaZero excels at strong play, it falls short of perfect play due to imperfect trajectory learning. Adding oracle-derived supervision via AZAL substantially enhances alignment with optimal strategies, demonstrating that targeted policy guidance can bridge the gap, though complete perfection remains elusive in some settings.

Abstract: AlphaZero has demonstrated that a neural-guided Monte Carlo Tree Search can achieve superhuman performance, but strong play does not necessarily imply perfect play. We study this gap in two oracle-evaluable domains with contrasting structure: Connect Four, a solved partisan game with exact game-theoretic values, and Chomp, an impartial game whose optimal play is governed by Grundy-number structure. Under a unified self-play $+$ MCTS pipeline, we compare vanilla AlphaZero, a multi-frame variant (limited to Chomp), and an AlphaZero Auxiliary Loss (AZAL) that adds oracle-derived policy supervision. We find that vanilla AlphaZero achieves strong play across both domains but cannot preserve the exact trajectories required for optimal play: in Connect Four, it fails to maintain the optimal line of play, while in Chomp, it fails to consistently restore the $g=0$ invariant. On rectangular Chomp boards, multi-frame inputs alone do not remove this gap. Nevertheless, AZAL substantially improves oracle consistency across multi-seeded full-game traces and sampled-state evaluations. On Chomp, AZAL reaches perfect full-game oracle consistency on 10x11 and high but not complete consistency on 9x10; on Connect Four, AZAL improves oracle-match rate and delays the first oracle mistake, but does not reach perfect play.

### [148] [Group Invariant Spectral Embedding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08987)
*Yeari Vigder,Paulina Hoyos,David Thong,Joakim andén,Joe Kileel,Amit Moscovich*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种将对称性融入谱嵌入亲和核的新方法，以解决标准谱嵌入在处理具有旋转等对称性的高维数据时忽略对称性的问题。通过在李群 $G$ 作用下的黎曼流形上构建 $G$-不变核，证明了图拉普拉斯算子收敛到商空间 $M/G$ 上的显式二阶微分算子，并实现了更优的收敛速率（因有效维度降低）。实验验证表明，该方法能准确恢复数据的内在几何结构，而传统方法即使在无限数据下也无法做到这一点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多实际数据集具有旋转等对称性，但标准谱嵌入方法未考虑这些对称性，导致对称相关点被误认为无关，影响降维与聚类效果。因此需要将对称性信息直接整合到嵌入过程中。

Method: 在具有紧李群 $G$ 对称性的黎曼流形 $M$ 上，构造三种类型的 $G$-不变亲和核，并分析基于这些核构建的图拉普拉斯算子在 $M/G$ 商空间上的渐近行为，证明其收敛至特定二阶微分算子。

Result: 理论证明了 $G$-不变核可使图拉普拉斯算子收敛到商空间上的明确微分算子，且收敛速度优于标准方法；实验显示该方法能正确恢复数据的内在几何结构，而标准方法失败。

Conclusion: 将对称性嵌入亲和核中，显著提升了谱嵌入在对称数据上的性能，不仅提高了收敛效率，还确保了内在几何结构的正确恢复，适用于 $\mathrm{SO}(2)$、$\mathrm{SO}(3)$ 等对称情形。

Abstract: Spectral embedding methods are widely used for dimensionality reduction and clustering of high-dimensional datasets with intrinsic low-dimensional structures. Although many datasets of practical interest exhibit invariance under symmetries such as rotations, standard spectral embedding methods do not account for this, treating symmetry-related data points as unrelated. Our approach to this problem is to incorporate the symmetries directly into the affinity kernels used for spectral embedding. We analyze the case of a Riemannian data manifold $M$ with symmetries given by a compact Lie group~$G$ and prove that, under suitable conditions, graph Laplacians constructed from three types of invariant kernels converge pointwise to explicit second-order differential operators on the quotient space $M/G$. Our analysis implies improved convergence rates, as the effective dimension drops according to the dimension of the group. We validate our approach on datasets with $\mathrm{SO}(2)$ or $\mathrm{SO}(3)$ symmetry, and show that $G$-invariant spectral embedding recovers the intrinsic geometry of the data, in contrast to standard spectral embedding, which fails to do so even in the limit of infinite data.

### [149] [Sensitivity-Aware Thresholding and Token Routing for Activation Sparsification in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08991)
*Bishmoy Paul,Youngmin Yi,Hoeseok Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究大语言模型（LLM）高效推理中的计算压缩问题，提出SATS方法通过敏感度感知的阈值校准替代传统的百分位数校准，以更精准地稀疏化MLP激活；同时引入轻量级的逐令牌动态路由框架，实现基于每个令牌的路径选择，而非全局应用修改。实验表明，SATS在相同稀疏度下优于基线，而令牌路由在质量与吞吐量之间提供了更优权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在保持模型质量的前提下，减少大语言模型推理过程中的计算开销是提升效率的关键挑战。现有方法依赖于固定的激活稀疏化策略，但阈值选择不够精细，且静态计算路径无法适应不同输入的复杂性，因此需要更智能的稀疏化和路由机制。

Method: 提出SATS（Sensitivity-Aware Thresholding for Sparsity），利用局部MLP输出敏感度代理来校准各层门控阈值，替代传统基于激活百分位数的方法；设计一种轻量级的令牌级条件路由机制，根据每个令牌动态决定走基础路径或优化路径。

Result: SATS在相同实际稀疏度下优于基准方法，显著提升了稀疏化效果；令牌路由相比静态激活修改方法，在模型质量与推理速度之间实现了更优的平衡，整体提升了质量-吞吐量权衡性能。

Conclusion: 改进的阈值校准方法与细粒度的令牌路由机制能够有效提升大语言模型的推理效率，为实现高性能、低延迟的LLM部署提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Efficient inference in Large Language Models (LLMs) requires deciding where computation can be reduced while preserving model quality. We study this problem through multilayer perceptron (MLP) activation sparsification and token-level conditional routing. We first propose Sensitivity-Aware Thresholding for Sparsity (SATS), a threshold calibration method to choose layerwise gate thresholds using a local MLP output sensitivity proxy rather than calibrating thresholds directly from activation percentiles. While SATS retains the existing mechanism of sparsifying MLP activations by thresholding gate activations, it replaces percentile-based calibration with a sensitivity-aware selection rule. We then introduce a lightweight token routing framework that dynamically selects between a base path and a modified path on a per-token basis, rather than applying the modified computation uniformly to all tokens. We evaluate both methods on multiple recent open-weight LLMs. Our results show that SATS improves over the threshold-based sparsification baseline at matched actual sparsity and that token routing yields a more favorable quality-throughput trade-off than static activation modification baselines. Overall, our results suggest that improved threshold calibration and token routing can improve the quality-throughput trade-off in LLMs.

Abstract: Graph Neural Networks have emerged as a powerful tool for the fast and accurate prediction of various crystal properties. Added to this, explicitly incorporating all chemical and structural features, that might influence a specific crystal property into the GNN encoder, is a challenging task. In this work, we propose a soft prompt learning framework that captures latent features essential for property prediction, which are not explicitly provided to the GNN. We introduce a novel multilevel graph prompt learning framework comprising both node-level and graph-level soft prompts. At the node level, we capture the local chemical semantics of different atom types, while at the graph level, we encode the global structural symmetry of the crystal graph. Method: 提出两种算法：1）耦合奖励混合方法，将真实奖励与代理奖励混合以加速学习；2）解耦预测混合方法，分别建模真实与代理奖励，并自适应组合其预测结果，增强对代理信号误设的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 所提方法能够有效利用代理奖励信号，在保证鲁棒性的同时实现更优的学习性能，适用于现实世界中存在相关动作与不完美代理信号的应用场景。

Abstract: We study contextual bandit problems with correlated arms and access to surrogate reward signals produced by a machine learning model, motivated by applications such as large language model (LLM) routing. Unlike classical contextual bandits that rely solely on bandit feedback and assume conditional independence across arms, our setting allows context-dependent inter-arm correlations and auxiliary reward information that may be noisy or misspecified. We propose algorithms that leverage such surrogate rewards through two complementary designs. A coupled reward-mixing approach pools true and surrogate rewards to accelerate learning when surrogate signals are reliable, while a decoupled prediction-mixing approach maintains separate estimators for bandit feedback and surrogate rewards and adaptively combines their predictions. This decoupling yields robustness to surrogate misspecification, recovering regret guarantees comparable to reward-only bandit methods in the worst case, while achieving improved regret when surrogate predictions are sufficiently informative. We provide theoretical regret analyses for both approaches and evaluate them on LLM routing benchmarks under varying accuracy versus cost trade-offs. The results demonstrate improved sample efficiency and consistently better accuracy-cost trade-offs compared to standard contextual bandit baselines and strong static routing methods.

Method: 引入广义泊松流（GPFlow），通过最小化负对数似然来学习非齐次广义泊松过程的速率函数，并建立群体层面的分布恢复保证及KL散度上界，支持多模态（欧氏、类别、黎曼）数据生成。

Abstract: The ability to generate variable-length proteins is crucial in protein design, where the optimal length is often unknown and tightly coupled to designability. To address this limitation, we introduce Generalized Poisson Flow (GPFlow), a variable-length generative framework that learns the rate function of an inhomogeneous generalized Poisson process by minimizing its negative log-likelihood. We establish population-level guarantees for recovering the joint multimodal distribution and derive an upper bound on the KL divergence between the data and generated distributions. We comprehensively evaluate GPFlow across structure and sequence design, motif scaffolding, and peptide co-design, spanning Euclidean, categorical, and Riemannian modalities to fully validate its variable-length generation quality. In unconditional design, GPFlow improves structural designability and achieves the best distributional fitness for sequence design compared to their corresponding fixed-length baselines, while perfectly recovering the length distribution. In conditional motif scaffolding, GPFlow ranks first on 10 of 16 structure-based design tasks with significantly more unique successes and also achieves more passed tasks in sequence-based design. In peptide co-design, GPFlow remains competitive even without access to a native-length oracle.

### [153] [Learning More from Less: Reinforcement Learning from Hindsight](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09042)
*Iris Xu,Sunshine Jiang,John Marangola,Nitish Dashora,Richard Li,Thomas Liu,Zexue He,Yuheng Zhi,Alex Pentland,Pulkit Agrawal,Zhang-Wei Hong*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出一种名为从事后学习（LfH）的新方法，通过将失败的机器人轨迹重新标注为实际完成的任务，提升视觉-语言-动作模型在强化学习后训练中的样本效率。该方法利用统一的视觉-语言模型重定义指令和奖励，使策略能从失败中学习，显著提升在分布外任务上的表现，尤其在稀疏奖励环境下效果突出。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在视觉-语言-动作模型的强化学习后训练中，由于机器人轨迹采集成本高且任务常提供稀疏奖励，导致策略早期频繁失败且难以学习。现有方法无法有效利用这些失败轨迹中的潜在信息。因此需要一种机制，将失败轨迹转化为可学习的成功经验，以提高样本效率。

Method: 提出学习从事后（LfH）方法，利用统一的视觉-语言模型对失败的轨迹进行事后重标注：自动生成新的指令并评估每个轨迹满足新指令的程度，将原任务与重标注后的任务联合用于训练，从而让策略从失败中学习。

Result: 在分布外的LIBERO-PRO任务上，标准RL方法进展缓慢，而LfH实现5倍的样本效率提升，并优于密集进度奖励基线。该方法在不同视觉-语言-动作模型架构上均有效，且在物理Franka机器人上验证成功。

Conclusion: LfH通过引入事后重标注机制，充分利用失败轨迹中的隐含信息，显著提升了视觉-语言-动作模型在稀疏奖励环境下的样本效率与泛化能力，为机器人强化学习提供了一种高效、通用的解决方案。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) is increasingly used to post-train vision-language-action (VLA) models, but every update consumes robot rollouts that are slow and costly to collect, making sample efficiency a central concern. Manipulation tasks typically provide only sparse rewards, so a weak policy fails almost every rollout early in training and has little to learn from, even when those failures execute coherent behavior. Such a failure, however, is a success at a different task. We present Learning from Hindsight (LfH), which brings hindsight relabeling to RL post-training of VLAs by scoring failed rollouts against the tasks they actually achieved. A single vision-language model relabels both the instruction and the reward, proposing a hindsight instruction for a group of failed rollouts and scoring how well each satisfies it, and the policy trains on the relabeled and original rollouts jointly. Because VLAs generalize across language, relabeling in language lets the policy learn more from the same trajectories. On out-of-distribution LIBERO-PRO tasks, where standard RL improves only slowly, LfH achieves $5\times$ improvement in sample efficiency, and outperforms a dense progress-reward baseline. The gains hold across VLA backbones and on a physical Franka robot.

### [154] [Super-Tuning: From Activation-Aware Pruning to Sparse Fine-Tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09287)
*Ivan Ilin,Philip Zmushko,Peter Richtárik*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了如何利用剪枝中发展的显著性信号来选择大语言模型微调时的参数更新位置，提出了一种名为Super的稀疏参数高效微调（PEFT）方法，通过Wanda风格的激活加权幅度分数确定一个小型可训练支持集。进一步提出Supra，一种结合稀疏更新与LoRA的混合适配器，通过简单的预算分割规则保持可训练参数总量不变。在Llama-3.2-1B和Meta-Llama-3-8B上的数学任务实验表明，Super/Supra表现最佳，且仅依赖幅度的固定支持集也具有有效性，说明基于剪枝思想的排序可为PEFT提供有效的稀疏支持，尤其与低秩适配器结合时效果更佳。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型微调成本高，因全参数更新需要大量内存、计算资源和每任务存储空间。现有方法难以在效率与性能间取得平衡。本文旨在探索是否可复用剪枝中的显著性信号，以指导高效、稀疏的参数更新，从而降低微调开销并提升效率。

Method: 提出Super方法：使用Wanda风格的激活加权幅度分数进行校准后，固定一小部分可训练参数作为支持集；提出Supra方法：将该稀疏更新与LoRA结合，通过预算分割规则控制总可训练参数量。实验采用单种子数学推理任务验证性能。

Result: 在Math17K算术任务上，Super和Supra的最佳变体在所有测试配置中达到最高平均准确率。同时，基于幅度的无训练基线（PaFi风格）也表现出良好性能，说明低分支持集在两种排序方式下均有效。

Conclusion: 基于剪枝启发的简单排序方法能够为参数高效微调提供有效的固定稀疏支持，尤其当与低秩适配器结合时，可在保持低计算开销的同时实现优异性能，为高效微调提供了新思路。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) remain expensive to fine-tune because full-parameter updates require substantial memory, compute, and per-task storage. We study whether saliency signals originally developed for pruning can be reused to choose where a model should adapt. We propose Super, a sparse parameter-efficient fine-tuning (PEFT) method that fixes a small trainable support using a Wanda-style activation-weighted magnitude score [Sun et al., 2023] computed from a calibration pass. We then introduce Supra, a hybrid adapter that combines this sparse update with LoRA while preserving a matched trainable-parameter budget through a simple budget-splitting rule. In single-seed Math17K arithmetic experiments on Llama-3.2-1B and Meta-Llama-3-8B, the best Super/Supra variants achieve the highest average accuracy among the tested schedule-selected adapter configurations. We also include a PaFi-style magnitude-only support as a closest training-free sparse baseline and find that low-score supports under both magnitude and Wanda-style orderings can be effective. These results suggest that simple pruning-inspired orderings can provide useful fixed sparse supports for PEFT, especially when combined with low-rank adapters.

### [155] [COBS: Cumulant Order Block Sparse Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09052)
*Alexander Tian,Aditya Ghai,Sanjit Neelam,Zaal Vasania,Akshay Mishra*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: COBS 提出一种基于累积量的块稀疏注意力方法，通过存储每块的压缩二阶统计量来更准确地近似注意力质量，显著提升长上下文任务性能，在32k RULER基准上将NSA基线得分从0.2999提升至0.8195，接近密集注意力（0.9040），仅需1.21倍KV缓存读取流量，远低于密集注意力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有块稀疏注意力方法因无法有效估计注意力质量而受限，尤其在长上下文场景中表现不佳，亟需更优的块选择策略以平衡性能与硬件效率。

Method: 提出COBS方法，利用累积量展开理论分析，突破一阶近似限制，引入二阶统计量压缩表示，实现对注意力质量更精准的近似。

Result: 在32k RULER长上下文检索任务中，COBS使NSA基线平均得分从0.2999提升至0.8195，接近密集注意力的0.9040，关闭约86%差距；同时仅需1.21倍于NSA的缓存读取开销，比密集注意力节省15.15倍；且保持短文本性能，负对数似然更低。

Conclusion: COBS通过高阶统计建模实现了高效且高质量的块稀疏注意力，为大模型长序列推理提供了可扩展、硬件友好的解决方案。

Abstract: Block sparse attention is a hardware friendly way to alleviate the key-value (KV) cache read bottleneck in large language models (LLMs). However, it is not prevalent among leading open-weight LLMs, which rely instead on dense attention or fine-grained selection, thereby motivating our analysis. We study DeepSeek's Native Sparse Attention (NSA) as a representative method, whose three-branch design lets us isolate block selection, the most challenging and consequential stage. We formalize selection and reduce it to ranking blocks by a single quantity, the attention mass: the sum of a block's attention scores. We show that if selection retrieves the blocks with the largest attention mass, block sparse attention can match the quality of dense attention. However, computing the exact attention mass requires reading every key, so the problem of block selection ultimately reduces to approximating this mass from a compact summary instead of the full keys. Via a cumulant expansion, we show why existing methods falter: their selection strategies attempt to estimate the attention mass, but are confined to a first-order approximation. Therefore, we propose COBS (Cumulant Order Block Sparse Attention), an attention method that builds on NSA, incorporating a novel selector that stores a compressed second-order statistic per block. On the 32k RULER long-context retrieval benchmark, COBS raises the NSA baseline's mean score from 0.2999 to 0.8195, approaching dense attention at 0.9040 and closing about 86% of the gap, while using only 1.21x the KV cache read traffic of the NSA baseline and 15.15x less read traffic than dense. The same model preserves short-context behavior and attains lower position-wise negative log-likelihood (NLL) than dense attention in our comparison.

### [156] [Mach-Mind-4-Flash Technical Report](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09375)
*Foundation Model Team*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Mach-Mind-4-Flash 是一个350亿参数的混合专家（MoE）代理模型，仅激活30亿参数。通过后训练优化，无需增加预训练计算量，其性能可媲美甚至超越1000亿参数级别的模型。该模型采用可扩展的代理交互环境进行大规模强化学习，显著提升了真实应用场景下的表现。整个流程分为三个阶段：(1) 统一的强化学习/操作员驱动训练基础设施，结合动态多教师调度和操作员级加速，实现17%的端到端训练速度提升；(2) 在推理、通用和代理三个领域并行训练多个专用强化学习专家，再通过多教师在线策略蒸馏（MOPD）融合为单一通用模型，采用路由反KL目标避免混合奖励强化学习中的性能波动问题；(3) 混合中位长度策略优化（HMPO），一种单阶段高效率方法，将推理链压缩19–46%，精度损失不超过0.7个百分点。该模型在AIME'26（92.70）、IFBench（82.82）、Behavioral-SafetyBench（80.74）、BFCL-v4（75.80）、BrowseComp-zh（72.31）和ClawBench（84.20）等基准上表现优异，性能领先或匹配激活参数量为其10–30倍的模型，且推理成本极低。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大模型在性能与计算成本之间存在巨大权衡，尤其在需要高效推理的现实应用中，高参数量模型难以部署。本文旨在通过高效的架构设计与训练策略，在不依赖大规模预训练计算的前提下，实现小激活规模模型达到接近甚至超越大模型的性能，从而降低推理成本，推动智能代理在真实场景中的落地应用。

Method: 提出Mach-Mind-4-Flash模型，采用350亿参数的混合专家（MoE）结构，仅激活30亿参数。通过三阶段训练流程：(1) 构建统一的强化学习/操作员驱动训练框架，支持动态多教师调度与操作员级加速，提升训练效率；(2) 多领域并行训练推理、通用和代理类强化学习专家，并利用多教师在线策略蒸馏（MOPD）融合为通用模型，使用路由反KL目标防止混合奖励训练中的性能退化；(3) 引入混合中位长度策略优化（HMPO），通过单阶段压缩推理链，减少冗余计算，保持高精度的同时提升效率。

Result: Mach-Mind-4-Flash在多个权威基准测试中表现卓越：AIME'26得分为92.70，IFBench为82.82，Behavioral-SafetyBench为80.74，BFCL-v4为75.80，BrowseComp-zh为72.31，ClawBench为84.20。其性能达到或超过激活参数量为其10–30倍的模型，同时推理成本仅为后者的极小部分，验证了其高效性与实用性。

Conclusion: Mach-Mind-4-Flash证明了通过后训练优化与创新的训练范式，可以在不增加预训练计算的情况下，实现小激活规模模型逼近甚至超越大模型的性能。其提出的多阶段训练框架、多教师蒸馏机制和高效推理压缩方法，为构建高性能、低成本的智能代理系统提供了新路径，具有重要的实用价值与推广潜力。

Abstract: We present Mach-Mind-4-Flash, a 35B-parameter Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) agentic model with 3B activated parameters. Through post-training optimization alone without scaling pre-training compute, the model achieves performance on par with or surpassing that of 100B-parameter-class models. By introducing scalable agentic interaction environments for large-scale reinforcement learning, the model attains significant performance gains on real-world application tasks. Our pipeline comprises three stages: (1) a unified RL/OPD training infrastructure with dynamic multi-teacher scheduling and operator-level acceleration, delivering 17\% end-to-end training speedup; (2) multiple domain-specific RL experts trained in parallel across Reasoning, General, and Agent tracks, then fused into a single generalist via Multi-Teacher On-Policy Distillation (MOPD) -- a routed reverse-KL objective that eliminates the see-saw degradation of mixed-reward RL; (3) Hybrid Median-length Policy Optimization (HMPO), a single-stage token-efficiency method that compresses reasoning chains by 19--46\% with $\le$0.7 percentage-point accuracy loss. Mach-Mind-4-Flash scores 92.70 on AIME'26, 82.82 on IFBench, 80.74 on Behavioral-SafetyBench, 75.80 on BFCL-v4, 72.31 on BrowseComp-zh, and 84.20 on ClawBench -- leading or matching models with 10--30$\times$ its activated size at a fraction of the inference cost.

Abstract: Edge devices are increasingly utilized for deploying deep learning applications on embedded systems. ### [158] [Neural Collapse Is Forbidden: Information Floors in Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09487)
*Bruno Abrahao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文探讨语言模型表示中的类内方差，认为其并非神经坍缩的不完全表现，而是信息存储的分配结果，并揭示了其遵循的规律。通过一个简化的中心化恒等式，推翻了以往关于单纯形等角紧框架的若干假设。研究发现，在14个模型中，宏观类别结构仅承载4-12%的表示方差，而词元上下文则占79-91%，且在参数量100倍变化范围内保持稳定。理论分析表明，词元级权重衰减会按类型数量而非出现频率惩罚类别，使下一个词预测转化为不平衡的K分类问题，最优解将类别范数按类型数量排序。进一步证明，对于二元类别存在下界，类内离散度至少与条件互信息I(token; context | category)成正比。实证结果表明：类内离散度（而非总方差）始终与信息量一致，无论在模型内部、跨模型之间，甚至在预训练过程中均成立，且一种模型的信息可预测另一种模型的离散度。预训练期间，类别方差占比先超调、下降并部分恢复，因所需携带的信息始终未丢失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解语言模型中类内方差的真实含义，挑战传统将其视为神经坍缩不完全的解释，提出其作为信息存储机制的全新视角，并建立理论与实证支持的统一规律。

Method: 结合数学恒等式推导、跨模型大规模实验分析、理论建模（如权重衰减影响）、信息论工具（条件互信息估计）、以及模型间与时间序列上的比较分析，采用无模型估计方法验证离散度与信息量的关系。

Result: 类内离散度是信息存储的关键指标，与条件互信息高度一致；宏观类别结构仅贡献少量方差（4-12%），上下文信息主导（79-91%）；跨模型和预训练过程中的方差动态可被信息量解释；权重衰减导致类别优化依类型数量而非频率。

Conclusion: 类内方差并非缺陷，而是信息存储的体现，其分布遵循‘身份离散度即信息量’的定律，该规律在多种模型和训练阶段均成立，为理解语言模型表征提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: Within-class variance in language-model representations is commonly read as incomplete neural collapse. We argue it is allocated information storage, and that the allocation obeys a law. A one-line centering identity voids a family of simplex equiangular-tight-frame claims, including our own earlier ones; in dimensionless variance shares across 14 models, macro-category structure carries only 4-12% of representational variance and within-token context carries 79-91%, stable across a 100x parameter range. On the theory side, token-level weight decay penalizes a category in proportion to its type count, not its occurrence mass, reducing next-token prediction to an imbalanced K-class problem whose optimum orders category norms by type count. A converse floor, proved for binary categories, forces within-category dispersion to be at least proportional to the conditional mutual information I(token; context | category). The law holds: identity dispersion, not total variance, tracks this information across every tested model and partition, under a model-free estimate and even across models, where one model's information predicts another's dispersion; and over pretraining the category share overshoots, decays, and partially recovers, because the information it must carry never left.

</details>


### [159] [Pitfalls and Remedies for Multi-Task Bayesian Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09073)
*Carl Hvarfner,Sam Daulton,Max Balandat,Eytan Bakshy*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了贝叶斯优化中多任务高斯过程作为默认转移学习方法的局限性，发现其在简单仿射相关任务中仍会错误估计跨任务相关性。问题源于两个结构机制：任务独立标准化引入有限样本对齐误差，而边际似然仅以每样本速率识别相关性，进一步被非重叠设计稀释。为此提出三种保守修正措施：将每任务均值和尺度设为模型参数、限制任务协方差为非负相关、部分共置源与目标设计点。这些改进在简单实例上恢复了单任务基线性能，但在更复杂实例及多数基于秩或潜在上下文的变体中仍存在失败。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多任务高斯过程是贝叶斯优化中常见的转移学习工具，但其在简单仿射相关任务中表现不佳，表明其存在根本性缺陷，亟需重新审视与改进。

Method: 通过控制实验分析多任务高斯过程在仿射相关任务中的表现，识别出导致相关性误估的两个结构性原因，并提出三种基于分析的修复策略。

Result: 所提方法在简单任务中可恢复单任务基线性能，但在复杂任务及多数变体中仍无法克服根本缺陷。

Conclusion: 多任务高斯过程在跨任务相关性建模上存在结构性缺陷，即使在理想条件下也难以准确捕捉真实关系；需谨慎使用并依赖更稳健的替代方案。

Abstract: Bayesian optimization routinely warm-starts a target experiment with data from related source tasks, and the multi-task Gaussian process is the textbook surrogate for the job. We revisit this default in a controlled setting and find that it misestimates the cross-task correlation even in the simplest non-trivial case, affinely related source and target tasks, where a working transfer learning method should obviously succeed. We trace the failure to two independent structural mechanisms. Per-task standardization, the textbook fix for the affine slice ambiguity, propagates a finite-sample alignment error into the recovered correlation. The marginal likelihood itself identifies the correlation only at a per-sample rate that a Gaussian process at non-overlapping designs further dilutes. We propose three conservative remedies that follow from the analysis: promoting per-task means and scales to model parameters, restricting the task covariance to non-negative correlations, and co-locating part of the source and target designs. Across synthetic multi-task problems and surrogate-based hyperparameter tuning transfer, these remedies recover the target-only baseline on the simple instances, while the broader failure persists on harder instances and across most rank-based and latent-context variants.

Beyond algorithmic improvements, we explore energy-efficient AI hardware, including mainstream AI chips, memory optimization, cross-platform deployment, and sustainable infrastructure. Furthermore, we examine how large models are being applied to sustainability-critical domains such as DeepSeek, remote sensing interpretation, national-scale infrastructure, and global initiatives. Finally, we discuss key challenges and future directions, highlighting the need for continual learning paradigms, memory-centric hardware, and standardized evaluation protocols. ### [161] [EXHOLD: Experience-Aware Real-Time Hold Control for Large-Scale Ride-Hailing Matching at DiDi](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09090)
*Xu Liu,Kai Wan,Zihao Lu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: EXHOLD 是一个可部署的两阶段框架，用于优化大规模网约车系统中的司机-订单匹配延迟控制。第一阶段通过统一目标函数学习决策模型，将司机-订单对分配到可解释的经验层级；第二阶段通过约束优化求解单调的持有时序，确保在不牺牲优质匹配的前提下最大化整体体验提升。在巴西滴滴生产环境的随机A/B测试中，EXHOLD显著提升了行程完成率、司机收入、市场效率，并大幅减少乘客取消行为，验证了其在时空异质性下的有效性与鲁棒性，目前已正式上线。
